      + "#" + BOX_ID + ":not(.km-collapsed) .km-arrow{transform:rotate(180deg);}"

      + "#" + BOX_ID + " .km-summary-content{padding:14px 16px;}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + " .km-summary-loading{font-size:13px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.82);line-height:1.7;}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + " .km-summary-item{font-size:14px;line-height:1.9;color:#fff;word-break:break-all;}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + " .km-summary-label{color:rgba(255,255,255,.72);margin-right:4px;}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + " .km-summary-detail{display:inline-block;margin-top:4px;color:#8dc4ff;text-decoration:none;font-size:14px;cursor:pointer;}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + " .km-summary-detail:hover{text-decoration:underline;}"

      + "#" + MASK_ID + "{"
      + "display:none;position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:999998;background:rgba(0,0,0,.12);"
      + "}"

      + "#" + PANEL_ID + "{"
      + "display:none;position:fixed;right:20px;bottom:20px;z-index:1000000;"
      + "width:520px;max-width:calc(100vw - 24px);overflow:auto;"
      + "border-radius:18px;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.14);"
      + "background:rgba(15,23,42,.28);"
      + "backdrop-filter:blur(18px);-webkit-backdrop-filter:blur(18px);"
      + "box-shadow:0 20px 50px rgba(0,0,0,.24);color:#fff;"
      + "font-family:Inter,-apple-system,BlinkMacSystemFont,'Segoe UI','PingFang SC','Microsoft YaHei',sans-serif;"
      + "}"

      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-head{display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;padding:14px 16px;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.1);}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-title{display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;font-size:15px;font-weight:700;}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-dot{width:10px;height:10px;border-radius:50%;background:#4da3ff;box-shadow:0 0 12px rgba(77,163,255,.9);display:inline-block;}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-close{border:none;background:rgba(255,255,255,.08);backdrop-filter:blur(12px);-webkit-backdrop-filter:blur(12px);color:#fff;width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:10px;cursor:pointer;font-size:16px;}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-body{padding:12px;}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-loading,#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-error{padding:18px 0;color:rgba(255,255,255,.86);text-align:center;}"

      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-card-wrap{text-align:center;}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-card-link{display:block;text-decoration:none;}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-card-image{display:block;width:100%;height:auto;border-radius:14px;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.12);background:rgba(255,255,255,.03);}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + " .km-card-tip{margin-top:10px;font-size:12px;line-height:1.7;color:rgba(255,255,255,.72);text-align:center;}"

      + "@media (max-width:640px){"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + "{right:12px;bottom:calc(12px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom));width:min(92vw,340px);max-width:none;}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + ".km-collapsed{width:auto;max-width:calc(100vw - 24px);}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + " .km-toggle{display:flex;}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + ".km-collapsed .km-summary-content{display:none;}"
      + "#" + BOX_ID + ":not(.km-collapsed) .km-summary-content{padding-top:0;padding-bottom:14px;}"
      + "#" + PANEL_ID + "{right:12px;left:12px;width:auto;max-width:none;}"
      + "}";

    var style = document.createElement("style");
    style.id = STYLE_ID;
    style.textContent = css;
    document.head.appendChild(style);
  }

  function createBase() {
    if (!byId(MASK_ID)) {
      var mask = document.createElement("div");
      mask.id = MASK_ID;
      document.body.appendChild(mask);
    }

    if (!byId(PANEL_ID)) {
      var panel = document.createElement("div");
      panel.id = PANEL_ID;
      panel.innerHTML =
        '<div class="km-head">'
        + '<div class="km-title"><span class="km-dot"></span><span>访问网络信息</span></div>'
        + '<button class="km-close" type="button">×</button>'
        + "</div>"
        + '<div class="km-body"><div class="km-loading">正在加载 IPPure Card...</div></div>';
      document.body.appendChild(panel);
    }

    if (!byId(BOX_ID)) {
      var box = document.createElement("div");
      box.id = BOX_ID;
      box.innerHTML =
        '<button type="button" class="km-toggle">'
        + '<span class="km-toggle-left"><span class="km-mini-dot"></span><span>网络信息</span></span>'
        + '<span class="km-arrow">⌃</span>'
        + "</button>"
        + '<div class="km-summary-content"><div class="km-summary-loading">正在获取网络信息...</div></div>';
      document.body.appendChild(box);
    }
  }

  function setBoxCollapsed(collapsed) {
    var box = byId(BOX_ID);
    if (!box) return;
    if (!isMobile()) {
      box.classList.remove("km-collapsed");
      return;
    }
    if (collapsed) {
      box.classList.add("km-collapsed");
    } else {
      box.classList.remove("km-collapsed");
    }
  }

  function positionPanel() {
    var panel = byId(PANEL_ID);
    var box = byId(BOX_ID);
    if (!panel || !box) return;

    var gap = 10;
    var rect = box.getBoundingClientRect();
    var bottom = window.innerHeight - rect.top + gap;
    var maxHeight = rect.top - gap - 12;

    if (isMobile()) {
      panel.style.left = "12px";
      panel.style.right = "12px";
      panel.style.width = "auto";
    } else {
      panel.style.left = "auto";
      panel.style.right = "20px";
      panel.style.width = "520px";
    }

    panel.style.bottom = bottom + "px";
    panel.style.maxHeight = Math.max(220, maxHeight) + "px";
  }

  function openPanel() {
    var panel = byId(PANEL_ID);
    var mask = byId(MASK_ID);

    if (isMobile()) setBoxCollapsed(true);
    positionPanel();

    if (panel) panel.style.display = "block";
    if (mask) mask.style.display = "block";
  }

  function closePanel() {
    var panel = byId(PANEL_ID);
    var mask = byId(MASK_ID);
    if (panel) panel.style.display = "none";
    if (mask) mask.style.display = "none";
  }

  function setSummaryError(msg) {
    var content = byId(BOX_ID).querySelector(".km-summary-content");
    if (!content) return;
    content.innerHTML = '<div class="km-summary-loading">' + text(msg) + "</div>";
  }

  function fetchJson(url) {
    return fetch(url, { cache: "no-store" }).then(function (res) {
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error("HTTP " + res.status);
      return res.json();
    });
  }

  function normalize(data) {
    if (data && data.success === false) throw new Error(data.message || "API error");

    return {
      ip: data.ip || data.query || "--",
      isp: data.connection && data.connection.isp ? data.connection.isp : (data.org || data.isp || "--"),
      asn: data.connection && data.connection.asn ? data.connection.asn : (data.asn || "--"),
      country: data.country || data.country_name || "--",
      region: data.region || data.region_name || "--",
      city: data.city || "--"
    };
  }

  function fetchInfo() {
    return fetchJson("https://ipwho.is/")
      .then(normalize)
      .catch(function () {
        return fetchJson("https://ipapi.co/json/").then(normalize);
      });
  }

  function loadSummaryData() {
    fetchInfo()
      .then(function (info) {
        cachedInfo = info;
        renderSummary(info);
      })
      .catch(function (err) {
        console.error("[komari net info summary]", err);
        setSummaryError("获取失败，请稍后刷新重试");
      });
  }

  function renderSummary(info) {
    var content = byId(BOX_ID).querySelector(".km-summary-content");
    if (!content) return;

    var countryRegion = [info.country, info.region, info.city]
      .filter(function (x) {
        return x && x !== "--";
      })
      .join(" / ") || "--";

    content.innerHTML =
      '<div class="km-summary-item"><span class="km-summary-label">国家地区：</span>' + text(countryRegion) + "</div>"
      + '<div class="km-summary-item"><span class="km-summary-label">运营商：</span>' + text(info.isp) + "</div>"
      + '<div class="km-summary-item"><span class="km-summary-label">IP：</span>' + text(info.ip) + "</div>"
      + '<div class="km-summary-item"><a href="javascript:void(0)" class="km-summary-detail">查看详情</a></div>';

    setBoxCollapsed(isMobile());
    positionPanel();
  }

  function renderCard() {
    var body = byId(PANEL_ID).querySelector(".km-body");
    if (!body) return;

    body.innerHTML =
      '<div class="km-card-wrap">'
      + '  <a class="km-card-link" href="https://ippure.com/MyIP-Info-Card.html" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">'
      + '    <img class="km-card-image" src="https://my.ippure.com/v1/card" alt="访客IP信息卡片" title="点击查看IP信息" />'
      + '  </a>'
      + '  <div class="km-card-tip">点击上方卡片可前往 IPPure 页面查看完整信息</div>'
      + '</div>';

    positionPanel();
  }

  function bind() {
    var panel = byId(PANEL_ID);
    var mask = byId(MASK_ID);
    var box = byId(BOX_ID);
    var closeBtn = panel.querySelector(".km-close");

    box.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
      var target = e.target;

      if (target && target.classList.contains("km-summary-detail")) {
        e.preventDefault();
        openPanel();
        renderCard();
        return;
      }

      var toggle = target.closest(".km-toggle");
      if (toggle && isMobile()) {
        e.preventDefault();
        box.classList.toggle("km-collapsed");
        positionPanel();
      }
    });

    mask.addEventListener("click", closePanel);
    closeBtn.addEventListener("click", closePanel);

    document.addEventListener("keydown", function (e) {
      if (e.key === "Escape") closePanel();
    });

    document.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
      if (!isMobile()) return;
      if (!box.contains(e.target) && byId(PANEL_ID).style.display !== "block") {
        setBoxCollapsed(true);
      }
    });

    window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
      setBoxCollapsed(isMobile());
      positionPanel();
    });
  }

  function init() {
    addStyle();
    createBase();
    bind();
    loadSummaryData();
  }

  if (document.readyState === "loading") {
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", init);
  } else {
    init();
  }
})();
</script></head>

<script>
  /* ═══ NanoMuse v1.3.1 — JS ═══ */
  ;(function(){
  'use strict';
  window._pageStart = performance.now();
  
  /* ══ Theme Toggle ══ */
  (function initTheme(){
    var savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('komari-theme');
    var prefersDark = window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
    var theme = savedTheme || (prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light');
    if(theme === 'dark') document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
    updateThemeLabel(theme);
  })();
  
  function updateThemeLabel(theme){
    var label = document.getElementById('themeLabel');
    if(label) label.textContent = theme === 'dark' ? 'DARK' : 'LIGHT';
  }
  
  window.toggleTheme = function(){
    var html = document.documentElement;
    var isDark = html.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'dark';
    if(isDark){
      html.removeAttribute('data-theme');
      localStorage.setItem('komari-theme', 'light');
      updateThemeLabel('light');
    } else {
      html.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
      localStorage.setItem('komari-theme', 'dark');
      updateThemeLabel('dark');
    }
  };
  
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    if(e.target.closest('#themeToggle')){
      window.toggleTheme();
    }
  });

/* ── State ── */
const S={
  nodes:[],liveData:{},onlineSet:new Set(),
  loggedIn:false,sitename:'KOMARI',themeSettings:{},
  groups:[],currentGroup:'ALL',searchTerm:'',
  ws:null,_wsI:null,wsRetries:0,
  _lastF:[],
  detailUUID:null,detailNode:null,detailHours:6,detailTab:'load',detailPingHours:6,detailWsData:[],
  VER:'v1.3.1',
  fleetLoadHist:[]
};
const STAB={hours:6,sort:'name',data:null,tasks:[],taskId:null,loading:false,_tasksFromApi:false};
window.S=S;window.STAB=STAB;

/* ── Utils ── */
const $=s=>document.getElementById(s);
const esc=s=>{const d=document.createElement('div');d.textContent=s;return d.innerHTML};
function fB(b,d=2){if(!b&&b!==0)return'--';const u=['B','KB','MB','GB','TB','PB'];let i=0;let v=Math.abs(b);while(v>=1024&&i<u.length-1){v/=1024;i++}return v.toFixed(i>0?d:0)+' '+u[i]}
function fS(bps){if(!bps&&bps!==0)return'--';const a=Math.abs(bps);if(a>=1073741824)return(a/1073741824).toFixed(2)+' GB/s';if(a>=1048576)return(a/1048576).toFixed(1)+' MB/s';if(a>=1024)return(a/1024).toFixed(1)+' KB/s';return a.toFixed(0)+' B/s'}
function fUs(s){if(!s)return'--';const d=Math.floor(s/86400),h=Math.floor((s%86400)/3600);return d>0?d+'d '+h+'h':h+'h'}
function fT(ts){if(!ts)return'--';const d=new Date(ts*1000);return d.toLocaleString('zh-CN',{month:'2-digit',day:'2-digit',hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'})}
function fTL(t){if(!t)return'--';const d=new Date(t);const M=String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0');const D=String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,'0');const h=String(d.getHours()).padStart(2,'0');const m=String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2,'0');return M+'/'+D+' '+h+':'+m}
function pc(u,t){if(!t)return 0;return Math.min(100,Math.round(u/t*100))}
function mColor(v){if(v>=80)return'red';if(v>=60)return'amber';if(v>=30)return'green';return'blue'}
function mH(label,value,isOff,hw){const c=isOff?'red':mColor(value);const v=isOff?value:Math.min(100,value);const hwHtml=hw?`<span class="nc-hw">${esc(hw)}</span>`:'';return`<div class="nc-m"><span class="nc-ml">${label}</span><div class="nc-mt"><div class="nc-mf ${c}" style="width:${v}%"></div></div><span class="nc-mv"${v>=80?' style="color:var(--r)"':''}>${Math.round(v)}%</span>${hwHtml}</div>`}
function uMt(card,label,value){const rows=card.querySelectorAll('.nc-m');for(const r of rows){if(r.querySelector('.nc-ml').textContent===label){const bar=r.querySelector('.nc-mf');const vEl=r.querySelector('.nc-mv');const v=Math.min(100,value);const c=mColor(v);bar.className='nc-mf '+c;bar.style.width=v+'%';vEl.textContent=Math.round(v)+'%';vEl.style.color=v>=80?'var(--r)':'';break}}}
function varHash(uuid){let h=0;for(let i=0;i<uuid.length;i++){h=((h<<5)-h)+uuid.charCodeAt(i);h|=0}return Math.abs(h)}
/* ── flatLive: convert nested WS/recent data → flat format for rendering ── */
function flatLive(r){
  if(!r||typeof r!=='object')return r;
  // Already flat? (has 'cpu' as number) — return as-is
  if(typeof r.cpu==='number')return r;
  return{
    cpu:Math.round((r.cpu?.usage||0)*100)/100,
    memory_used:r.ram?.used||0, memory_total:r.ram?.total||0,
    swap_used:r.swap?.used||0, swap_total:r.swap?.total||0,
    disk_used:r.disk?.used||0, disk_total:r.disk?.total||0,
    network_tx:r.network?.up||0, network_rx:r.network?.down||0,
    network_total_up:r.network?.totalUp||0, network_total_down:r.network?.totalDown||0,
    tcp:r.connections?.tcp||0, udp:r.connections?.udp||0,
    load1:r.load?.load1||0, load5:r.load?.load5||0, load15:r.load?.load15||0,
    uptime:r.uptime||0, process:r.process||0,
    os:r.os||'', message:r.message||'', updated_at:r.updated_at||''
  };
}
/* Stub functions — must keep */
function varDecoHTML(vr,on){return''}
function offlineDecoHTML(atk){return''}
function illustHTML(uuid){return''}

/* ── Offline fake data ── */
const FAKE_OS=['Quantum OS 12.0','NeuroLinux 25','ArcOS 7.7','HyperDebian 15','CrystalBSD 4.0','Void Engine 3.2'];
const FAKE_CPU=['AMD EPYC 9B84 256-Core','Intel Xeon w9-5690X 128-Core','Ampere Altra Q256-80','NVIDIA Grace 144-Core ARM','Qualcomm Oryon X1 96-Core','RISC-V SG2380 128-Core'];
const FAKE_MEM=[137438953472,274877906944,549755813888,1099511627776];
const FAKE_DSK=[2199023255552,4398046511104,8796093022208,17592186044416];

S._fakeCache={};
function genFake(uuid){
  if(S._fakeCache[uuid])return S._fakeCache[uuid];
  const s=varHash(uuid);
  const isAtk=((s>>7)&1)===0;
  const r=(min,max)=>min+((s^(min*7+max*13))%(max-min));
  if(isAtk){
    return{atk:true,cpu:r(55,96),ram:r(35,73),disk:r(20,56),
      tcp:r(5000,30000),udp:r(1000,8000),proc:r(2000,8000),
      netUp:r(52428800,1073741824),netDn:r(83886080,1073741824),
      os:FAKE_OS[s%FAKE_OS.length],cpuModel:FAKE_CPU[s%FAKE_CPU.length],
      mem:FAKE_MEM[s%FAKE_MEM.length],dsk:FAKE_DSK[s%FAKE_DSK.length]}
  }
  return{atk:false,cpu:Math.min(100,r(88,106)),ram:Math.min(100,r(85,103)),disk:Math.min(100,r(78,100)),
    tcp:r(200,700),udp:r(10,70),proc:r(800,1300),
    netUp:r(1024,51200),netDn:r(1024,51200),
    os:FAKE_OS[s%FAKE_OS.length],cpuModel:FAKE_CPU[s%FAKE_CPU.length],
    mem:FAKE_MEM[s%FAKE_MEM.length],dsk:FAKE_DSK[s%FAKE_DSK.length]}
}

/* ── API ── */
async function fetchP(){
  try{const r=await fetch('/api/public');const j=await r.json();const d=j.data||j;
    S.sitename=d.sitename||'KOMARI';S.themeSettings=d.theme_settings||{};
    S.recordRetention=d.record_preserve_time||720;
    S.pingRetention=d.ping_record_preserve_time||720;
    $('siteName').textContent=S.sitename;$('footerSite').textContent=S.sitename+' MONITOR';
    if(S.themeSettings.version_tag)S.VER=S.themeSettings.version_tag;
    S._alertCPU=parseInt(S.themeSettings.alert_cpu)||80;
    S._alertRAM=parseInt(S.themeSettings.alert_ram)||80;
    S._alertDISK=parseInt(S.themeSettings.alert_disk)||90;
    $('verBadge').textContent=S.VER;

    /* Apply theme settings: char_url, bg_video, announce, footer */
    const ts = S.themeSettings;
    if(ts.char_url){
      const ci=document.getElementById('charImg');
      if(ci) ci.src = ts.char_url;
    }
    if(ts.bg_video){
      const vb=document.getElementById('videoBg');
      const v=document.getElementById('bgVideo');
      const ab=document.getElementById('animeBg');
      if(v && vb){
        v.src = ts.bg_video;
        const vop = parseFloat(ts.bg_video_opacity)||0.7;
        /* After charReveal (4.5s) finishes, wait for video then crossfade */
        const elapsed=performance.now()-window._pageStart;
        const wait=Math.max(0,5000-elapsed);
        setTimeout(()=>{
          function crossfade(){
            vb.style.opacity=vop;
            if(ab){ab.dataset.videoHidden='1';ab.style.cssText+='animation:none !important;transition:opacity 1.5s ease !important;opacity:0 !important'}
          }
          if(v.readyState>=3){crossfade();return}
          v.oncanplay=()=>crossfade();
        },wait);
      }
    }
    if(ts.footer_text){
      const fe=document.getElementById('footerSite');
      if(fe) fe.textContent = ts.footer_text;
    }
    if(ts.announce_text){
      const ae=document.getElementById('announceBar');
      if(ae){ae.textContent=ts.announce_text;ae.style.display='block'}
    }
  }catch(e){console.warn('fetchP:',e)}
}
async function fetchN(){
  try{const r=await fetch('/api/nodes');const j=await r.json();const d=j.data||j;
    S.nodes=(Array.isArray(d)?d:[]).sort((a,b)=>(a.weight||0)-(b.weight||0));
    const gs=new Set();S.nodes.forEach(n=>{if(n.group)gs.add(n.group)});
    S.groups=['ALL',...gs];
  }catch(e){console.warn('fetchN:',e)}
}
async function fetchMe(){
  try{const r=await fetch('/api/me');const j=await r.json();const d=j.data||j;S.loggedIn=!!d.logged_in}catch(e){}
}
function conWS(){
  try{
    const p=location.protocol==='https:'?'wss:':'ws:';
    S.ws=new WebSocket(p+'//'+location.host+'/api/clients');
    S.ws.onopen=()=>{S.wsRetries=0;S.ws.send('get');$('wsStatus').textContent='UPDATING ...';$('sysLink').textContent='ACTIVE';$('rightStatus').textContent='STATUS — ACTIVE';if(S._wsPoll)clearInterval(S._wsPoll);S._wsPoll=setInterval(()=>{if(S.ws&&S.ws.readyState===1)S.ws.send('get')},3000)};
    S.ws.onmessage=e=>{
      try{const m=JSON.parse(e.data);
        /* Match PRTS exactly: server sends {status:'success',data:{online:[],data:{}}} */
        let payload=null;
        if(m.status==='success'&&m.data){
          /* Standard Komari envelope */
          payload=m.data;
        }else if(Array.isArray(m.online)){
          /* Raw payload without status wrapper */
          payload=m;
        }else if(m.data&&Array.isArray(m.data.online)){
          /* data wrapper without status field */
          payload=m.data;
        }
        if(!payload){console.warn('[NM] WS unknown format',Object.keys(m));return}
        S.onlineSet=new Set(payload.online||[]);
        /* Clear fake cache for nodes that came online */
        if(S._fakeCache){S.onlineSet.forEach(function(u){delete S._fakeCache[u]})}
        if(payload.data&&typeof payload.data==='object'){
          for(const[k,v]of Object.entries(payload.data))S.liveData[k]=flatLive(v);
        }
        uCards();rSum();uCharEyes();
        /* Cleanup stale liveData for removed nodes */
        if(S.nodes.length>0){const validUuids=new Set(S.nodes.map(n=>n.uuid));for(const k in S.liveData){if(!validUuids.has(k))delete S.liveData[k]}}
        if(S.detailUUID)uDetLive();
        if(document.querySelector('#pg-worldmap.active')&&typeof initWorldMap==='function'){if(!S._wmInited){initWorldMap();S._wmInited=true}else if(typeof wmapUpdateNodes==='function'){wmapUpdateNodes()}}
      }catch(er){console.error('[NM]',er)}
    };
    S.ws.onclose=()=>{if(S._wsPoll)clearInterval(S._wsPoll);$('wsStatus').textContent='RECONNECT ...';reWS()};
    S.ws.onerror=()=>{S.ws.close()};
  }catch(e){reWS()}
}
function reWS(){
  if(S._wsI)return;
  S._wsI=setTimeout(()=>{S._wsI=null;S.wsRetries++;conWS()},Math.min(3000*Math.pow(1.5,S.wsRetries),30000));
}

/* ── Filter ── */
function gF(){
  return S.nodes.filter(n=>{
    if(n.hidden&&!S.loggedIn)return false;
    if(S.currentGroup!=='ALL'&&n.group!==S.currentGroup)return false;
    if(S.searchTerm){const t=S.searchTerm.toLowerCase();if(!((n.name||'').toLowerCase().includes(t)||(n.region||'').toLowerCase().includes(t)))return false}
    return true;
  });
}

/* ── Character Eyes: awake when all online, asleep when any offline ── */
function uCharEyes(){
  var total=S.nodes.filter(function(n){return !n.hidden}).length;
  var allOn=total>0&&S.onlineSet.size>=total;
  var ts=S.themeSettings||{};
  var state=allOn?'awake':'sleep';
  if(S._charState===state)return;
  S._charState=state;

  var ci=document.getElementById('charImg');
  var vb=document.getElementById('videoBg');
  var v=document.getElementById('bgVideo');
  var ab=document.getElementById('animeBg');

  if(allOn&&ts.bg_video_awake){
    /* All online + awake video configured → show awake video */
    if(v&&vb){
      v.src=ts.bg_video_awake;
      v.load();
      var vop=parseFloat(ts.bg_video_opacity)||0.7;
      function showAwakeVideo(){vb.style.opacity=vop;if(ab){ab.style.cssText+='transition:opacity 0.8s;opacity:0 !important'}}
      if(v.readyState>=3){showAwakeVideo()}else{v.oncanplay=showAwakeVideo}
    }
  }else if(allOn){
    /* All online + no awake video → show awake image */
    if(ci){
      var awakeUrl=ts.char_awake_url||'./char-awake.png';
      ci.src=awakeUrl;
    }
    /* Hide video if it was playing, show character */
    if(vb)vb.style.opacity='0';
    if(ab){ab.style.cssText='';ab.removeAttribute('data-video-hidden')}
  }else{
    /* Has offline → show default sleep state */
    if(ts.bg_video&&v&&vb){
      /* Restore default video */
      v.src=ts.bg_video;
      v.load();
      var vop2=parseFloat(ts.bg_video_opacity)||0.7;
      function showSleepVideo(){vb.style.opacity=vop2;if(ab){ab.style.cssText+='transition:opacity 0.8s;opacity:0 !important'}}
      if(v.readyState>=3){showSleepVideo()}else{v.oncanplay=showSleepVideo}
    }else{
      /* No video → show sleep image */
      if(ci){
        var sleepUrl=ts.char_url||'./char.png';
        ci.src=sleepUrl;
      }
      if(vb)vb.style.opacity='0';
      if(ab){ab.style.cssText='';ab.removeAttribute('data-video-hidden')}
    }
  }
}

/* ── Render Summary (Hero panels) ── */
function rSum(){
  const fl=gF();const total=fl.length;
  let onC=0,cpuS=0,ramS=0,diskS=0,netS=0,peakCpu=0,bwUp=0,bwDn=0,onN=0;
  fl.forEach(n=>{
    const on=S.onlineSet.has(n.uuid);
    const d=S.liveData[n.uuid];
    if(on&&d){
      onC++;
      const cpu=d.cpu||0,ram=d.memory_used&&d.memory_total?pc(d.memory_used,d.memory_total):0;
      const disk=d.disk_used&&d.disk_total?pc(d.disk_used,d.disk_total):0;
      cpuS+=cpu;ramS+=ram;diskS+=disk;
      if(cpu>peakCpu)peakCpu=cpu;
      bwUp+=(d.network_tx||0);bwDn+=(d.network_rx||0);
    }
  });
  const offC=total-onC;onN=onC||1;
  const avgCpu=Math.round(cpuS/onN),avgRam=Math.round(ramS/onN),avgDisk=Math.round(diskS/onN);
  $('hAvgCpu').textContent=avgCpu+'%';$('hAvgRam').textContent=avgRam+'%';$('hPeak').textContent=Math.round(peakCpu)+'%';
  /* Fleet Health Score: 100 minus weighted resource usage (CPU 40%, RAM 35%, Disk 25%) */
  const healthScore=total&&onC?Math.max(0,Math.min(100,
    100-(avgCpu*0.4+avgRam*0.35+avgDisk*0.25)
  )).toFixed(1):'--';
  $('hScore').textContent=healthScore;
  /* Sync Ring */
  const syncEl=$('syncRing');const syncPctEl=$('syncPct');
  if(syncEl&&total){const pct=onC/total*100;const circ=2*Math.PI*88;syncEl.style.strokeDashoffset=(circ-(circ*pct/100)).toFixed(1);if(syncPctEl)syncPctEl.textContent=pct.toFixed(0)+'%'}
  /* Fleet Strip */
  const fT=$('fTotal');if(fT)fT.textContent=total;
  const fU=$('fUprate');if(fU)fU.textContent=total?(onC/total*100).toFixed(1)+'%':'--';
  const fA=$('fAlerts');if(fA)fA.textContent=offC;
    const tl=$('threatLevel');if(tl){if(offC>=5){tl.textContent='HIGH';tl.className='threat-level high'}else if(offC>=2){tl.textContent='MEDIUM';tl.className='threat-level medium'}else{tl.textContent='LOW';tl.className='threat-level low'}}
  const fL=$('fAvgLoad');if(fL)fL.textContent=avgCpu+'%';
  updateFleetCost();
  /* Hero bars */
  const setBar=(id,vid,v)=>{const e=$(id);if(e)e.style.width=Math.min(100,v)+'%';const ve=$(vid);if(ve)ve.textContent=Math.round(v)+'%'};
  setBar('heroBarCpu','heroValCpu',avgCpu);
  setBar('heroBarRam','heroValRam',avgRam);
  setBar('heroBarDisk','heroValDisk',avgDisk);
  /* Active nodes & alerts */
  const hAN=$('hActiveN');if(hAN)hAN.textContent=onC;
  const hAL=$('hAlertN');if(hAL)hAL.textContent=offC;
  /* Top pressure: which resource is highest */
  const hTP=$('hTopPressure');
  if(hTP){const pressures=[{n:'CPU',v:avgCpu},{n:'RAM',v:avgRam},{n:'DISK',v:avgDisk}];pressures.sort((a,b)=>b.v-a.v);hTP.textContent=pressures[0].n}
  /* Bandwidth display */
  const fSplit=fS(bwUp).split(' ');$('hNetUp').textContent=fSplit[0];$('hNetUpU').textContent=fSplit[1]||'MB/s';
  const fSplit2=fS(bwDn).split(' ');$('hNetDn').textContent=fSplit2[0];$('hNetDnU').textContent=fSplit2[1]||'MB/s';

  /* ── Alert Atmosphere System (3 layers) ── */
  const hasAlert=offC>0;

  /* Layer 3: Global atmosphere — body class toggle */
  if(hasAlert&&!document.body.classList.contains('alert-active')){
    document.body.classList.add('alert-active');
  }else if(!hasAlert&&document.body.classList.contains('alert-active')){
    document.body.classList.remove('alert-active');
  }

  /* Layer 2: Fleet strip ALERTS cell pulse */
  const alertCell=document.querySelector('.fleet-cell:nth-child(3)');
  if(alertCell){
    if(hasAlert&&!alertCell.classList.contains('alert-pulse')){alertCell.classList.add('alert-pulse')}
    else if(!hasAlert&&alertCell.classList.contains('alert-pulse')){alertCell.classList.remove('alert-pulse')}
  }

  /* Layer 3 bonus: Core ring visual shift handled by CSS body.alert-active .sr-fill */

  /* ── Fleet INTERNAL LOAD live waveform ── */
  const avgLoad=(avgCpu+avgRam)/2;
  S.fleetLoadHist.push(avgLoad);
  if(S.fleetLoadHist.length>60)S.fleetLoadHist.shift();
  const flc=$('fleetLoadCanvas');
  if(flc){
    const dpr=window.devicePixelRatio||1;
    const rect=flc.parentElement.getBoundingClientRect();
    const w=rect.width,h=rect.height;
    if(flc.width!==Math.round(w*dpr)||flc.height!==Math.round(h*dpr)){flc.width=Math.round(w*dpr);flc.height=Math.round(h*dpr)}
    const ctx=flc.getContext('2d');
    ctx.setTransform(dpr,0,0,dpr,0,0);
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,w,h);
    const pts=S.fleetLoadHist;
    if(pts.length>1){
      const maxV=Math.max(50,...pts)*1.2;
      const stepX=w/(pts.length-1);
      /* Fill */
      ctx.beginPath();
      ctx.moveTo(0,h);
      for(let i=0;i<pts.length;i++){
        const x=i*stepX,y=h-(pts[i]/maxV)*h*0.85;
        if(i===0)ctx.lineTo(x,y);
        else{const px=(i-1)*stepX,py=h-(pts[i-1]/maxV)*h*0.85;ctx.bezierCurveTo(px+stepX*0.4,py,x-stepX*0.4,y,x,y)}
      }
      ctx.lineTo(w,h);ctx.closePath();
      const grad=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,h);
      grad.addColorStop(0,'rgba(56,189,248,0.18)');grad.addColorStop(1,'rgba(56,189,248,0.02)');
      ctx.fillStyle=grad;ctx.fill();
      /* Line */
      ctx.beginPath();
      for(let i=0;i<pts.length;i++){
        const x=i*stepX,y=h-(pts[i]/maxV)*h*0.85;
        if(i===0)ctx.moveTo(x,y);
        else{const px=(i-1)*stepX,py=h-(pts[i-1]/maxV)*h*0.85;ctx.bezierCurveTo(px+stepX*0.4,py,x-stepX*0.4,y,x,y)}
      }
      ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(56,189,248,0.55)';ctx.lineWidth=1.5;ctx.stroke();
    }
  }
}

/* ── Render Cards ── */
function rCards(fl){
  if(!fl)fl=gF();
  /* Sort: offline/alert nodes first for visibility */
  fl.sort((a,b)=>{const aOn=S.onlineSet.has(a.uuid)?1:0;const bOn=S.onlineSet.has(b.uuid)?1:0;if(aOn!==bOn)return aOn-bOn;return(a.weight||0)-(b.weight||0)});
  const c=$('nodeCards');if(!c)return;
  const uuids=fl.map(n=>n.uuid);
  S._lastF=uuids;
  let html='';
  fl.forEach((n,i)=>{
    const on=S.onlineSet.has(n.uuid);
    let d=S.liveData[n.uuid];
    let fake=null;
    if(!on){fake=genFake(n.uuid);d=d||{}}
    const cpu=on?(d.cpu||0):(fake?fake.cpu:0);
    const ram=on&&d.memory_used&&d.memory_total?pc(d.memory_used,d.memory_total):(fake?fake.ram:0);
    const disk=on&&d.disk_used&&d.disk_total?pc(d.disk_used,d.disk_total):(fake?fake.disk:0);
    const health=on?Math.max(0,Math.round(100-(cpu+ram+disk)/3)):0;
    const hc=health>60?'g':health>30?'am':'r';
    const circ=2*Math.PI*21;const off=circ-(circ*health/100);
    const netUp=on?fS(d.network_tx||0):'--';
    const netDn=on?fS(d.network_rx||0):'--';
    const totalUp=on?fB(d.network_total_up||0,1):'--';
    const totalDn=on?fB(d.network_total_down||0,1):'--';
    const uptime=on&&d.uptime?fUs(d.uptime):'--';

    /* Hardware info (meter 末尾) */
    const hwCpu=on?(n.cpu_cores||'?')+' Cores':(fake?(fake.cpuModel?fake.cpuModel.split(' ')[0]+'+':'? Cores'):'');
    const hwRam=on?fB(d.memory_total||n.mem_total||0,0):(fake?fB(fake.mem||0,0):'');
    const hwDisk=on?fB(d.disk_total||n.disk_total||0,0):(fake?fB(fake.dsk||0,0):'');

    /* SYS / CPU 型号 / MEM / DISK 精确值 / TOTAL */
    const osStr=on?(d.os||n.os||'--'):(fake?fake.os:'--');
    const cpuModel=on?(d.cpu_model||n.cpu_name||n.cpu_model||'--'):(fake?fake.cpuModel||'--':'--');
    const memStr=on&&d.memory_used&&d.memory_total?(fB(d.memory_used,1)+' / '+fB(d.memory_total,1)):'-- / --';
    const diskStr=on&&d.disk_used&&d.disk_total?(fB(d.disk_used,1)+' / '+fB(d.disk_total,1)):'-- / --';

    /* 连接数 + 进程数 */
    const tcpN=on?(d.tcp_conn_count||d.tcp||0):'--';
    const udpN=on?(d.udp_conn_count||d.udp||0):'--';
    const procN=on?(d.process||d.proc_count||0):'--';
    const fmtK=v=>{if(typeof v!=='number')return v;if(v>=10000)return(v/1000).toFixed(1)+'k';return v.toString()};

    /* 区域 chips */
    const region=n.region||'';const group=n.group||'';
    const chips=[];
    if(region)chips.push('<span class="nc-chip" style="color:var(--cyan);border-color:var(--cyan-border);background:var(--cyan-soft)">'+esc(region)+'</span>');
    if(group)chips.push('<span class="nc-chip">'+esc(group)+'</span>');

    /* 套餐信息(parseLabels + fBilling) */
    const labels=parseLabels(n);
    const bandwidth=labels.bandwidth||'';
    const traffic=labels.traffic||'';
    const ipVer=n.ipv6==false?'V4':(n.ipv4==false?'V6':'V4');
    const bill=(typeof fBilling==='function')?fBilling(n):{str:'',monthly:0,currency:''};
    /* 剩余天数 */
    let daysLeft='';let daysLeftCls='';
    if(n.expired_at){
      const ed=new Date(n.expired_at);const nw=new Date();
      const days=Math.ceil((ed-nw)/(1000*60*60*24));
      if(days>0){
        daysLeft='余 '+days+' 天';
        daysLeftCls=days<=7?' danger':days<=30?' warn':'';
      }else if(days===0){
        daysLeft='今日到期';daysLeftCls=' danger';
      }else{
        daysLeft='已过期 '+(-days)+' 天';daysLeftCls=' danger';
      }
    }

    /* 套餐条:永远渲染,缺字段用占位(保证卡片高度一致) */
    let pkgHtml='<div class="nc-pkg">';
    pkgHtml+='<span class="nc-pkg-chip">'+ipVer+'</span>';
    pkgHtml+=bandwidth?'<span class="nc-pkg-chip bw">'+esc(bandwidth)+'</span>':'<span class="nc-pkg-chip ph">—</span>';
    pkgHtml+=traffic?'<span class="nc-pkg-chip tr">'+esc(traffic)+'</span>':'<span class="nc-pkg-chip ph">—</span>';
    pkgHtml+='<div class="nc-pkg-price">';
    if(bill.str){
      pkgHtml+='<span><span class="price">'+esc(bill.str.split('/')[0])+'</span><span class="cycle"> / '+esc(bill.str.split('/')[1]||'')+'</span></span>';
    }else{
      pkgHtml+='<span class="ph-price">—</span>';
    }
    if(daysLeft){
      pkgHtml+='<span class="left'+daysLeftCls+'">'+daysLeft+'</span>';
    }else{
      pkgHtml+='<span class="left ph-left">—</span>';
    }
    pkgHtml+='</div></div>';

    /* 状态标签 / HUD */
    const offCls=on?'':(fake&&fake.atk?'off atk':'off ovl');
    const dly=Math.min(9,Math.floor(i/2)+4);
    const secTag='SEC-'+String.fromCharCode(65+Math.floor(i/4));
    const nodeNum=String(i+1).padStart(2,'0');
    const statusTag=on?'ONLINE · LINK OK':(fake&&fake.atk?'OFFLINE · UNDER ATTACK':'OFFLINE · OVERLOAD');
    const badgeCls=on?'on':(fake&&fake.atk?'off':'alert');
    const badgeText=on?'ONLINE':(fake&&fake.atk?'OFFLINE':'ALERT');
    const dotCls=on?'on':(fake&&fake.atk?'off':'warn');
    const uuidShort=(n.uuid||'').slice(0,8).toUpperCase();
    const offMsg=fake&&fake.atk?'UNDER ATTACK':'OVERLOAD';

    html+=`<div class="nc ${offCls} an d${dly}" data-uuid="${n.uuid}" onclick="openDet('${n.uuid}')">
      <div class="nc-c tl"></div><div class="nc-c tr"></div><div class="nc-c bl"></div><div class="nc-c br"></div>
      <div class="nc-scan"></div>
      <div class="nc-hud">
        <div class="nc-hud-text">NODE.${nodeNum}<br><b>${secTag}</b></div>
        <div class="nc-hud-sig"><span></span><span></span><span></span></div>
      </div>
      <div class="nc-h">
        <div class="nc-h-l">
          <div class="nc-tag"><span class="nc-dot ${dotCls}"></span>${statusTag}</div>
          <div class="nc-n">${esc(n.name||n.uuid)}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="nc-badge ${badgeCls}">${badgeText}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="nc-uuid-line"><span class="line l"></span><span>UUID · <b>${uuidShort}</b></span><span class="line r"></span></div>
      <div class="nc-meta">${chips.length?chips.join(''):'<span class="nc-chip ph">—</span>'}</div>
      ${pkgHtml}
      <div class="nc-body">
        <div class="nc-ring">
          <svg viewBox="0 0 52 52">
            <circle class="nc-ring-halo ${hc}" cx="26" cy="26" r="21"/>
            <circle class="nc-ring-bg" cx="26" cy="26" r="21"/>
            <circle class="nc-ring-fg ${hc}" cx="26" cy="26" r="21" stroke-dasharray="${circ.toFixed(1)}" stroke-dashoffset="${off.toFixed(1)}"/>
          </svg>
          <div class="nc-ring-val" style="color:var(--${hc})">${on?health:'--'}</div>
          <div class="nc-ring-lbl">HEALTH</div>
        </div>
        <div class="nc-meters">${mH('CPU',cpu,!on,hwCpu)}${mH('RAM',ram,!on,hwRam)}${mH('DISK',disk,!on,hwDisk)}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="nc-sys">
        <div class="nc-sys-h"><span class="sl"></span>SYSTEM INFO<span class="sl"></span></div>
        <div class="nc-sys-g">
          <div class="nc-sys-r"><span class="k">SYS</span><span class="v" data-sys="os">${esc(osStr)}</span></div>
          <div class="nc-sys-r"><span class="k">CPU</span><span class="v" data-sys="cpu">${esc(cpuModel)}</span></div>
          <div class="nc-sys-r"><span class="k">MEM</span><span class="v" data-sys="mem">${memStr}</span></div>
          <div class="nc-sys-r"><span class="k">DISK</span><span class="v" data-sys="disk">${diskStr}</span></div>
          <div class="nc-sys-r"><span class="k">TOTAL</span><span class="v" data-sys="total">${on?`<span class="au">↑</span> ${totalUp} <span style="color:var(--t4);margin:0 6px">|</span> <span class="ad">↓</span> ${totalDn}`:'<span style="opacity:.4">↑ -- | ↓ --</span>'}</span></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="nc-nc">
        <span class="up"${on?'':' style="opacity:.4"'}>↑ ${netUp}</span>
        <span class="dn"${on?'':' style="opacity:.4"'}>↓ ${netDn}</span>
        <div class="conn">
          <span>TCP<b data-conn="tcp">${fmtK(tcpN)}</b></span>
          <span>UDP<b data-conn="udp">${fmtK(udpN)}</b></span>
          <span>PROC<b data-conn="proc">${fmtK(procN)}</b></span>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="nc-hbar"><span class="nc-hbar-lbl">HP</span>${(function(){let b='';for(let i=0;i<20;i++){const filled=i<(on?Math.ceil(health/5):0);const isWarn=i>=16;let cls='';if(filled){cls=isWarn?' warn':(health>=90?' g':health>=70?' a':' r')}b+='<div class="nc-hblk'+cls+'"></div>'}return b})()}<span class="nc-hbar-up${on&&uptime!=='--'?'':' ph'}" data-fd="up">${on&&uptime!=='--'?`UP ${uptime}`:'UP --'}</span></div>
      ${on?'':`<div class="nc-f-off"><span>⚠ &nbsp;${offMsg}</span><span>LINK LOST</span></div>`}
    </div>`;
  });
  c.innerHTML=html;
}

/* ── Update Cards (WS incremental) — v1.2.0 ── */
function uCards(){
  const fl=gF();const newUuids=fl.map(n=>n.uuid);
  const same=newUuids.length===S._lastF?.length&&newUuids.every(u=>S._lastF.includes(u));
  if(!same){rCards(fl);return}
  fl.forEach(n=>{
    const card=document.querySelector(`.nc[data-uuid="${n.uuid}"]`);if(!card)return;
    const on=S.onlineSet.has(n.uuid);
    const d=S.liveData[n.uuid]||{};
    let cpu,ram,disk;
    const fakeN=!on?genFake(n.uuid):null;
    if(on){
      cpu=d.cpu||0;ram=d.memory_used&&d.memory_total?pc(d.memory_used,d.memory_total):0;
      disk=d.disk_used&&d.disk_total?pc(d.disk_used,d.disk_total):0;
    }else{
      cpu=fakeN.cpu;ram=fakeN.ram;disk=fakeN.disk;
    }
    uMt(card,'CPU',cpu);uMt(card,'RAM',ram);uMt(card,'DISK',disk);

    /* Health ring — halo + main */
    const health=on?Math.max(0,Math.round(100-(cpu+ram+disk)/3)):0;
    const hc=health>60?'g':health>30?'am':'r';
    const circ=2*Math.PI*21;const offDash=circ-(circ*health/100);
    const halo=card.querySelector('.nc-ring-halo');
    if(halo)halo.setAttribute('class','nc-ring-halo '+hc);
    const ring=card.querySelector('.nc-ring-fg');
    if(ring){ring.setAttribute('class','nc-ring-fg '+hc);ring.setAttribute('stroke-dashoffset',offDash.toFixed(1))}
    const rv=card.querySelector('.nc-ring-val');
    if(rv){rv.textContent=on?health:'--';rv.style.color='var(--'+hc+')'}

    /* HP 条 — v1.2.0 最后 4 格警戒色 */
    const hblks=card.querySelectorAll('.nc-hblk');
    if(hblks.length===20){
      for(let i=0;i<20;i++){
        const filled=i<(on?Math.ceil(health/5):0);
        const isWarn=i>=16;
        let cls='nc-hblk';
        if(filled){cls+=isWarn?' warn':(health>=90?' g':health>=70?' a':' r')}
        hblks[i].className=cls;
      }
    }

    /* UPTIME in HP bar */
    let upEl=card.querySelector('.nc-hbar-up');
    if(on&&d.uptime){
      const upStr=fUs(d.uptime);
      if(!upEl){
        upEl=document.createElement('span');upEl.className='nc-hbar-up';upEl.setAttribute('data-fd','up');
        card.querySelector('.nc-hbar')?.appendChild(upEl);
      }
      upEl.textContent='UP '+upStr;
    }else if(upEl){upEl.remove()}

    /* Net + TCP/UDP/PROC (合并行) */
    const ncEl=card.querySelector('.nc-nc');
    if(ncEl){
      const spans=ncEl.querySelectorAll(':scope > span.up, :scope > span.dn');
      if(spans.length>=2){
        spans[0].textContent='↑ '+(on?fS(d.network_tx||0):'--');
        spans[1].textContent='↓ '+(on?fS(d.network_rx||0):'--');
        if(on){spans[0].style.opacity='';spans[1].style.opacity=''}
        else{spans[0].style.opacity='.4';spans[1].style.opacity='.4'}
      }
      const fmtK=v=>{if(typeof v!=='number')return v;if(v>=10000)return(v/1000).toFixed(1)+'k';return v.toString()};
      const tcpB=ncEl.querySelector('[data-conn="tcp"]');
      const udpB=ncEl.querySelector('[data-conn="udp"]');
      const procB=ncEl.querySelector('[data-conn="proc"]');
      if(tcpB)tcpB.textContent=on?fmtK(d.tcp_conn_count||d.tcp||0):'--';
      if(udpB)udpB.textContent=on?fmtK(d.udp_conn_count||d.udp||0):'--';
      if(procB)procB.textContent=on?fmtK(d.process||d.proc_count||0):'--';
    }

    /* SYSTEM INFO 块更新(SYS/CPU/MEM/DISK/TOTAL) */
    const sysOs=card.querySelector('[data-sys="os"]');
    if(sysOs)sysOs.textContent=on?(d.os||n.os||'--'):(fakeN?fakeN.os:'--');
    const sysCpu=card.querySelector('[data-sys="cpu"]');
    if(sysCpu)sysCpu.textContent=on?(d.cpu_model||n.cpu_name||n.cpu_model||'--'):(fakeN?fakeN.cpuModel||'--':'--');
    const sysMem=card.querySelector('[data-sys="mem"]');
    if(sysMem){
      if(on&&d.memory_used&&d.memory_total)sysMem.textContent=fB(d.memory_used,1)+' / '+fB(d.memory_total,1);
      else sysMem.textContent='-- / --';
    }
    const sysDisk=card.querySelector('[data-sys="disk"]');
    if(sysDisk){
      if(on&&d.disk_used&&d.disk_total)sysDisk.textContent=fB(d.disk_used,1)+' / '+fB(d.disk_total,1);
      else sysDisk.textContent='-- / --';
    }
    const sysTotal=card.querySelector('[data-sys="total"]');
    if(on&&sysTotal){
      const tUp=fB(d.network_total_up||0,1);
      const tDn=fB(d.network_total_down||0,1);
      sysTotal.innerHTML='<span class="au">↑</span> '+tUp+' <span style="color:var(--t4);margin:0 6px">|</span> <span class="ad">↓</span> '+tDn;
    }else if(!on){
      const sysTotalRow=card.querySelector('.nc-sys-r:last-child [data-sys="total"]');
      if(sysTotalRow)sysTotalRow.closest('.nc-sys-r').style.display='none';
    }

    /* Hardware info 末尾(cores/mem/disk) */
    const hwSpecs=on
      ?[(n.cpu_cores||'?')+' Cores',fB(d.memory_total||n.mem_total||0,0),fB(d.disk_total||n.disk_total||0,0)]
      :[(n.cpu_cores||'?')+' Cores',fakeN&&fakeN.mem?fB(fakeN.mem,0):'',fakeN&&fakeN.dsk?fB(fakeN.dsk,0):''];
    card.querySelectorAll('.nc-m').forEach((mrow,idx)=>{
      mrow.querySelectorAll('.nc-hw').forEach(e=>e.remove());
      const hw=document.createElement('span');hw.className='nc-hw';
      hw.textContent=hwSpecs[idx]||'';
      mrow.appendChild(hw);
    });

    /* 状态 dot / badge / tag */
    const dotCls=on?'on':(fakeN&&fakeN.atk?'off':'warn');
    const dot=card.querySelector('.nc-dot');
    if(dot)dot.setAttribute('class','nc-dot '+dotCls);
    const badge=card.querySelector('.nc-badge');
    if(badge){
      const bcls=on?'on':(fakeN&&fakeN.atk?'off':'alert');
      const btext=on?'ONLINE':(fakeN&&fakeN.atk?'OFFLINE':'ALERT');
      badge.setAttribute('class','nc-badge '+bcls);badge.textContent=btext;
    }
    const tag=card.querySelector('.nc-tag');
    if(tag){
      const statusTxt=on?'ONLINE · LINK OK':(fakeN&&fakeN.atk?'OFFLINE · UNDER ATTACK':'OFFLINE · OVERLOAD');
      tag.innerHTML='<span class="nc-dot '+dotCls+'"></span>'+statusTxt;
    }

    /* Card root class */
    if(on){card.classList.remove('off','atk','ovl')}else{
      card.classList.add('off');
      card.classList.toggle('atk',!!(fakeN&&fakeN.atk));
      card.classList.toggle('ovl',!(fakeN&&fakeN.atk));
    }

    /* Off footer */
    let offFooter=card.querySelector('.nc-f-off');
    if(!on){
      const offMsg=fakeN&&fakeN.atk?'UNDER ATTACK':'OVERLOAD';
      if(!offFooter){
        offFooter=document.createElement('div');offFooter.className='nc-f-off';
        card.appendChild(offFooter);
      }
      offFooter.innerHTML='<span>⚠ &nbsp;'+offMsg+'</span><span>LINK LOST</span>';
    }else if(offFooter){offFooter.remove()}

    /* Alert threshold highlights */
    if(on){
      card.classList.toggle('alert-cpu',cpu>=(S._alertCPU||80));
      card.classList.toggle('alert-ram',ram>=(S._alertRAM||80));
      card.classList.toggle('alert-disk',disk>=(S._alertDISK||90));
    }else{card.classList.remove('alert-cpu','alert-ram','alert-disk')}
  });
}

/* ── Group filter ── */
function rGF(){
  const c=$('groupPills');if(!c)return;
  let h=S.groups.map(g=>`<button class="pill${g===S.currentGroup?' a':''}" data-g="${esc(g)}">${esc(g)}</button>`).join('');
  h+='<button class="pill" style="margin-left:auto;opacity:.7" onclick="nav(\'/stability\')">◈ STABILITY</button>';
  h+='<button class="pill" style="opacity:.7" onclick="nav(\'/worldmap\')">◈ MAP</button>';
  h+='<button class="pill" style="opacity:.7" onclick="nav(\'/billing\')">◈ BILLING</button>';
  c.innerHTML=h;
  c.querySelectorAll('.pill[data-g]').forEach(b=>{
    b.onclick=()=>{S.currentGroup=b.dataset.g;rGF();rCards()}
  });
}

/* ── Detail Page ── */
window.openDet=function(uuid){
  S.detailUUID=uuid;
  S.detailNode=S.nodes.find(n=>n.uuid===uuid);
  S.detailTab='load';S.detailHours=6;S.detailPingHours=6;S.detailWsData=[];
  nav('/detail/'+uuid);
};
function rDetInfo(node,uuid){
  const on=S.onlineSet.has(uuid);
  const _plDet=parseLabels(node);
  const d=S.liveData[uuid]||{};
  const c=$('detContent');if(!c)return;
  const cpu=Math.round(d.cpu||0),ram=d.memory_total?Math.round(pc(d.memory_used||0,d.memory_total)):0;
  const disk=d.disk_total?Math.round(pc(d.disk_used||0,d.disk_total)):0;
  const swap=d.swap_total?Math.round(pc(d.swap_used||0,d.swap_total)):0;
  const health=on?Math.max(0,Math.round(100-(cpu*0.4+ram*0.35+disk*0.25))):0;
  /* Status grading */
  function statusGrade(h){if(!on)return{text:'OFFLINE',cls:'offline'};if(h>=80)return{text:'ACTIVE',cls:'st-active'};if(h>=60)return{text:'STABLE',cls:'st-stable'};if(h>=40)return{text:'WARNING',cls:'st-warning'};return{text:'CRITICAL',cls:'st-critical'}}
  const grade=statusGrade(health);
  function gaugeColor(v){return v>=80?'var(--r)':v>=50?'var(--am)':'var(--blue)'}
  function gaugeHex(v){return v>=80?'#ff4d4f':v>=50?'#eab308':'#2563eb'}
  /* Half-arc gauge: 180° arc — COLD ENERGY HUD version */
  function halfArc(val,color,hexC,label){
    /* v1.2.1 · full ring (matches node card ring language) */
    const v=Math.min(100,val);
    const r=42;const cx=54;const cy=54;
    const circ=2*Math.PI*r;
    const off=circ-(circ*v/100);

    /* Color: cold palette matching node card */
    const fillColor=v>=85?'rgba(160,140,200,0.9)':v>=70?'var(--am)':'var(--g)';
    const glowColor=v>=85?'rgba(160,140,200,0.55)':v>=70?'rgba(var(--amr),0.55)':'rgba(var(--gr),0.55)';
    const haloColor=v>=85?'rgba(160,140,200,0.14)':v>=70?'rgba(var(--amr),0.14)':'rgba(var(--gr),0.14)';

    const warnCls=v>=80?'highlight':v>=60?'warning':'';
    const valColor=on&&v>=85?'rgba(140,120,180,0.95)':on&&v>=70?'var(--am)':'var(--t)';

    return`<div class="det-gauge ${warnCls}">
      <div class="dc tl"></div><div class="dc tr"></div><div class="dc bl"></div><div class="dc br"></div>
      <div class="det-gauge-arc"><svg viewBox="0 0 108 108">
        <circle class="det-ga-halo" cx="${cx}" cy="${cy}" r="${r}" style="stroke:${haloColor}"/>
        <circle class="det-ga-ring-out" cx="${cx}" cy="${cy}" r="${r+8}"><animateTransform attributeName="transform" type="rotate" from="0 ${cx} ${cy}" to="360 ${cx} ${cy}" dur="18s" repeatCount="indefinite"/></circle>
        <circle class="det-ga-ring-in" cx="${cx}" cy="${cy}" r="${r-10}"><animateTransform attributeName="transform" type="rotate" from="360 ${cx} ${cy}" to="0 ${cx} ${cy}" dur="12s" repeatCount="indefinite"/></circle>
        <circle class="det-ga-bg" cx="${cx}" cy="${cy}" r="${r}"/>
        <circle class="det-ga-fill" cx="${cx}" cy="${cy}" r="${r}" style="stroke:${fillColor};stroke-dasharray:${circ.toFixed(1)};stroke-dashoffset:${on?off.toFixed(1):circ.toFixed(1)};filter:drop-shadow(0 0 6px ${glowColor})"/>
      </svg>
      <div class="det-gauge-val" style="color:${valColor}">${on?v:'--'}<span class="det-gauge-unit">%</span></div>
      </div>
    <div class="det-gauge-lbl">${label}</div>
    <div class="det-gauge-range"><span>0</span><span>50</span><span>100</span></div></div>`}

  /* ── Status Strip — v1.2.1 HUD redesign ── */
  const nodeNumDs='N.'+(uuid.slice(0,4).toUpperCase());
  const secDs='SEC-'+(uuid.charCodeAt(0)%4===0?'A':uuid.charCodeAt(0)%4===1?'B':uuid.charCodeAt(0)%4===2?'C':'D');
  let html=`<div class="det-strip">
    <div class="dc tl"></div><div class="dc tr"></div><div class="dc bl"></div><div class="dc br"></div>
    <div class="det-strip-scan"></div>
    <div class="det-strip-hud">
      <div class="det-strip-hud-t">${nodeNumDs}<br><b>${secDs}</b></div>
      <div class="det-strip-hud-sig"><span></span><span></span><span></span></div>
    </div>
    <div class="ds-cell ds-name"><div class="ds-name-v"><span class="ds-dot ${on?'on':'off'}"></span>${esc(node.name||uuid)}</div><div class="ds-name-uuid">UUID · <b>${esc(uuid.slice(0,8).toUpperCase())}</b></div></div>
    <div class="ds-cell"><div class="ds-k">STATUS</div><div class="ds-v ${on?'online':'offline'}">${on?'ONLINE':'OFFLINE'}</div></div>
    <div class="ds-cell"><div class="ds-k">GRADE</div><div class="ds-v ${grade.cls}">${grade.text}</div></div>
    <div class="ds-cell"><div class="ds-k">HEALTH</div><div class="ds-v ds-health" style="color:${on?(health>=80?'var(--g)':health>=60?'var(--cyan)':health>=40?'var(--am)':'var(--r)'):'var(--t4)'}">${on?health+'%':'--'}</div></div>
    <div class="ds-cell"><div class="ds-k">LATENCY</div><div class="ds-v" style="color:var(--cyan)">--</div></div>
    <div class="ds-cell"><div class="ds-k">PACKET LOSS</div><div class="ds-v" style="color:var(--cyan)">--</div></div>
    <div class="det-core-echo"><svg viewBox="0 0 36 36"><circle cx="18" cy="18" r="16" class="dce-ring"/><circle cx="18" cy="18" r="11" class="dce-inner"/><circle cx="18" cy="18" r="2" class="dce-dot"/></svg></div>
  </div>`;

  /* ── Half-Arc Gauges ── */
  /* ── Half-Arc Gauges (system priority order: CPU > DISK > RAM > SWAP) ── */
  html+=`<div class="det-gauges">
    ${halfArc(cpu,gaugeColor(cpu),gaugeHex(cpu),'CPU')}
    ${halfArc(disk,gaugeColor(disk),gaugeHex(disk),'DISK')}
    ${halfArc(ram,gaugeColor(ram),gaugeHex(ram),'RAM')}
    ${halfArc(swap,gaugeColor(swap),gaugeHex(swap),'SWAP')}
  </div>`;
  /* Billing info */
  var bInfo=fBilling(node);
  /* Info panels */
  html+=`<div class="det-panels">
    <div class="det-panel">
      <div class="dc tl"></div><div class="dc tr"></div><div class="dc bl"></div><div class="dc br"></div>
      <div class="det-panel-title">SYSTEM INFO</div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">REGION</span><span class="det-row-v">${esc(node.region||'--')}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">GROUP</span><span class="det-row-v">${esc(node.group||'--')}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">OS</span><span class="det-row-v">${esc(d.os||node.os||'--')}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">UPTIME</span><span class="det-row-v" style="color:${on?'var(--g)':'var(--t4)'}">${on?fUs(d.uptime):'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">CPU MODEL</span><span class="det-row-v">${esc(node.cpu_name||node.cpu_model||'--')}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">CORES</span><span class="det-row-v">${node.cpu_cores||'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">BANDWIDTH</span><span class="det-row-v" style="color:var(--cyan);font-weight:600">${_plDet.bandwidth||'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">TRAFFIC</span><span class="det-row-v" style="color:var(--cyan);font-weight:600">${_plDet.traffic||'不限'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">MONTHLY</span><span class="det-row-v" style="color:var(--cyan);font-weight:700">${bInfo.monthly>0?bInfo.currency+bInfo.monthly.toFixed(2):'--'}</span></div>
    </div>
    <div class="det-panel">
      <div class="dc tl"></div><div class="dc tr"></div><div class="dc bl"></div><div class="dc br"></div>
      <div class="det-panel-title">RESOURCES</div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">CPU</span><span class="det-row-v"${on&&cpu>=80?' style="color:var(--r)"':''}>${on?cpu+'%':'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">RAM</span><span class="det-row-v"${on&&ram>=80?' style="color:var(--r)"':''}>${on?fB(d.memory_used||0)+' / '+fB(d.memory_total||0):'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">SWAP</span><span class="det-row-v">${on?fB(d.swap_used||0)+' / '+fB(d.swap_total||0):'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">DISK</span><span class="det-row-v"${on&&disk>=80?' style="color:var(--r)"':''}>${on?fB(d.disk_used||0)+' / '+fB(d.disk_total||0):'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">NET ↑</span><span class="det-row-v" style="color:var(--g)">${on?fS(d.network_tx||0):'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">NET ↓</span><span class="det-row-v" style="color:var(--cyan)">${on?fS(d.network_rx||0):'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">TOTAL ↑</span><span class="det-row-v">${on?fB(d.network_total_up||0,1):'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">TOTAL ↓</span><span class="det-row-v">${on?fB(d.network_total_down||0,1):'--'}</span></div>
      <div class="det-row"><span class="det-row-k">TCP/UDP</span><span class="det-row-v">${on?(d.tcp_conn_count||d.tcp||0)+' / '+(d.udp_conn_count||d.udp||0):'--'}</span></div>
    </div>
  </div>`;
  html+=`<div class="det-tabs"><button class="det-tab${S.detailTab==='load'?' a':''}" data-t="load">LOAD</button><button class="det-tab${S.detailTab==='ping'?' a':''}" data-t="ping">PING</button></div>`;
  html+=`<div class="det-time" id="detTimeRow"></div>`;
  html+=`<div id="detCharts"></div>`;
  c.innerHTML=html;
  c.querySelectorAll('.det-tab').forEach(b=>{
    b.onclick=()=>{S.detailTab=b.dataset.t;rDetInfo(node,uuid);ldDetData()}
  });
  ldDetData();
}
function genTimeSteps(maxH){
  var all=[1,3,6,12,24,48,72,168,336,720];
  var steps=all.filter(function(h){return h<=maxH});
  if(steps.length===0||steps[steps.length-1]<maxH)steps.push(maxH);
  if(steps.length<=5)return steps;
  var pick=[steps[0]];var gap=(steps.length-1)/4;
  for(var i=1;i<4;i++)pick.push(steps[Math.round(i*gap)]);
  pick.push(steps[steps.length-1]);
  var unique=[];pick.forEach(function(v){if(unique.indexOf(v)===-1)unique.push(v)});
  return unique.sort(function(a,b){return a-b});
}
function fmtH(h){if(h<24)return h+'h';var d=Math.round(h/24);return d+'d'}
async function ldDetData(){
  const uuid=S.detailUUID;if(!uuid)return;
  const hours=S.detailTab==='load'?S.detailHours:S.detailPingHours;
  /* Time row */
  const tr=$('detTimeRow');
  if(tr){
    const maxH=S.detailTab==='load'?(S.recordRetention||720):(S.pingRetention||720);
    const steps=genTimeSteps(maxH);
    tr.innerHTML=steps.map(h=>`<button class="${h===hours?'a':''}" data-h="${h}">${fmtH(h)}</button>`).join('');
    tr.querySelectorAll('button').forEach(b=>{
      b.onclick=()=>{
        if(S.detailTab==='load')S.detailHours=+b.dataset.h;else S.detailPingHours=+b.dataset.h;
        ldDetData();
      }
    });
  }
  const cc=$('detCharts');if(!cc)return;
  cc.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:var(--t4)">Loading...</div>';
  try{
    if(S.detailTab==='load'){
      const r=await fetch(`/api/records/load?uuid=${uuid}&hours=${hours}`);const j=await r.json();const dd=j.data||j;
      rLoadCharts(dd.records||[]);
    }else{
      const r=await fetch(`/api/records/ping?uuid=${uuid}&hours=${hours}`);const j=await r.json();const dd=j.data||j;
      rPingCharts(dd);
      /* Update strip LATENCY + PACKET LOSS from ping records */
      uDetPingStrip(dd);
    }
  }catch(e){cc.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:var(--r)">Failed to load data</div>'}
  /* Always try to fetch latest ping for strip even on load tab */
  if(S.detailTab==='load'){try{
    const pr=await fetch(`/api/records/ping?uuid=${uuid}&hours=1`);const pj=await pr.json();const pd=pj.data||pj;
    uDetPingStrip(pd);
  }catch(e){}}
}
function uDetPingStrip(pd){
  const records=pd.records||[];
  if(!records.length)return;
  const strip=document.querySelector('#pg-detail .det-strip');
  if(!strip)return;
  const cells=strip.querySelectorAll('.ds-cell');
  /* LATENCY cell is index 4 (0:name 1:status 2:grade 3:health 4:latency 5:loss) */
  const validPings=records.filter(r=>r.value>=0);
  if(validPings.length&&cells[4]){
    const last=validPings[validPings.length-1];
    const vEl=cells[4].querySelector('.ds-v');
    if(vEl)vEl.textContent=last.value.toFixed(1)+' ms';
  }
  /* PACKET LOSS */
  if(records.length&&cells[5]){
    const total=records.length;
    const lost=records.filter(r=>r.value<0||r.value===null||r.value===undefined).length;
    const lossPct=((lost/total)*100).toFixed(1);
    const vEl=cells[5].querySelector('.ds-v');
    if(vEl)vEl.textContent=lossPct+'%';
  }
}
function rLoadCharts(records){
  const cc=$('detCharts');if(!cc||!records.length){cc.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:var(--t4)">No data</div>';return}
  /* Debug: log first record keys to understand API format */
  if(records[0])console.log('[NM] Load record sample:',JSON.stringify(records[0]));
  cc.innerHTML=`<div class="det-charts-grid">
    <div class="chart-wrap"><div class="chart-label">CPU %</div><canvas id="chCpu"></canvas></div>
    <div class="chart-wrap"><div class="chart-label">NETWORK</div><canvas id="chNet"></canvas></div>
  </div>`;
  /* Sort records by time ascending */
  records.sort((a,b)=>{const ta=new Date(a.time||a.timestamp||0).getTime();const tb=new Date(b.time||b.timestamp||0).getTime();return ta-tb});
  const labels=records.map(r=>{const t=r.time||r.timestamp;return fTL(t)});
  const rawTimes=records.map(r=>{const t=r.time||r.timestamp;return t?new Date(t).getTime():0});
  /* CPU: Komari may return 0-100 or 0-1 decimal — check max of first 20 samples */
  const cpuSamples=records.slice(0,20).map(r=>r.cpu||0);
  const cpuMax=Math.max(...cpuSamples);
  const cpuIsDecimal=cpuMax>0&&cpuMax<=1;
  const cpuData=records.map(r=>{let v=r.cpu||0;if(cpuIsDecimal)v=v*100;return Math.round(v*10)/10});
  dCh('chCpu',{labels,rawTimes,data:cpuData,color:'#2563eb',max:100,label:'%'});
  dCh('chNet',{labels,rawTimes,data:records.map(r=>(r.net_out||0)/1048576),color:'#00d2ff',label:'MB/s'});
}
function rPingCharts(pd){
  const cc=$('detCharts');if(!cc)return;
  const records=pd.records||[];
  const tasks=pd.tasks||[];
  if(!records.length){cc.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:var(--t4)">No ping data</div>';return}
  /* Group records by task_id */
  const PING_COLORS=['#2563eb','#00d2ff','#34d399','#a78bfa'];
  if(tasks.length>1){
    /* Multiple monitoring servers — one chart per task */
    const byTask=new Map();
    tasks.forEach(t=>byTask.set(t.id,{name:t.name||('Task '+t.id),records:[]}));
    records.forEach(r=>{
      const tid=r.task_id;
      if(tid!==undefined&&byTask.has(tid)){byTask.get(tid).records.push(r)}
      else if(!byTask.size){/* fallback */}
    });
    let html='<div class="det-charts-grid">';
    let idx=0;
    byTask.forEach((v,tid)=>{
      if(!v.records.length)return;
      const cid='chPing'+tid;
      /* Compute current value + loss rate for header */
      const last=v.records[v.records.length-1];
      const curVal=last&&last.value>=0?last.value.toFixed(1):'--';
      const total=v.records.length;
      const lost=v.records.filter(r=>r.value<0||r.value===null).length;
      const lossPct=total>0?((lost/total)*100).toFixed(1):'--';
      html+=`<div class="chart-wrap"><div class="chart-label"><span>▎LATENCY (ms)</span><span style="float:right;font-size:12px;opacity:.7">${esc(v.name)}</span></div><div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:0 8px;margin-bottom:4px;font-size:11px;opacity:.6"><span>Current: ${curVal} ms</span><span>Loss: ${lossPct}%</span></div><canvas id="${cid}"></canvas></div>`;
      idx++;
    });
    html+='</div>';
    cc.innerHTML=html;
    idx=0;
    byTask.forEach((v,tid)=>{
      if(!v.records.length)return;
      v.records.sort((a,b)=>new Date(a.time||0).getTime()-new Date(b.time||0).getTime());
      const cid='chPing'+tid;
      const labels=v.records.map(r=>fTL(r.time));
      const rawTimes=v.records.map(r=>{const t=r.time;return t?new Date(t).getTime():0});
      dCh(cid,{labels,rawTimes,data:v.records.map(r=>r.value>=0?r.value:0),color:PING_COLORS[idx%PING_COLORS.length],label:'ms'});
      idx++;
    });
  }else{
    /* Single task or no task info — original single chart */
    cc.innerHTML=`<div class="chart-wrap"><div class="chart-label">▎LATENCY (ms)${tasks.length?'<span style="float:right;font-size:12px;opacity:.7">'+esc(tasks[0].name)+'</span>':''}</div><canvas id="chPing"></canvas></div>`;
    records.sort((a,b)=>new Date(a.time||0).getTime()-new Date(b.time||0).getTime());
    const labels=records.map(r=>fTL(r.time));
    const rawTimes=records.map(r=>{const t=r.time;return t?new Date(t).getTime():0});
    dCh('chPing',{labels,rawTimes,data:records.map(r=>r.value>=0?r.value:0),color:'#2563eb'});
  }
}
function uDetLive(){
  if(!S.detailUUID||document.querySelector('#pg-detail').style.display==='none')return;
  const d=S.liveData[S.detailUUID];
  if(!d)return;
  const on=S.onlineSet.has(S.detailUUID);
  /* Update half-arc gauges */
  const gauges=document.querySelectorAll('#pg-detail .det-gauge');
  const cpu=Math.round(d.cpu||0),ram=d.memory_total?Math.round(pc(d.memory_used||0,d.memory_total)):0;
  const disk=d.disk_total?Math.round(pc(d.disk_used||0,d.disk_total)):0;
  const swap=d.swap_total?Math.round(pc(d.swap_used||0,d.swap_total)):0;
  const vals=[cpu,disk,ram,swap]; /* order matches gauge layout: CPU > DISK > RAM > SWAP */
  const r=60;const arcLen=Math.PI*r;
  gauges.forEach((g,i)=>{
    const v=Math.min(100,vals[i]||0);const off=arcLen-(arcLen*v/100);
    const fill=g.querySelector('.det-ga-fill');
    const vEl=g.querySelector('.det-gauge-val');
    const color=v>=80?'var(--r)':v>=50?'var(--am)':'var(--blue)';
    if(fill){fill.style.strokeDashoffset=on?off.toFixed(1):arcLen.toFixed(1);fill.style.stroke=color}
    if(vEl){if(!vEl.querySelector('.det-gauge-unit')){vEl.innerHTML=v+'<span class="det-gauge-unit">%</span>'}else{vEl.firstChild.textContent=on?v:'--'};vEl.style.color=on&&v>=80?'var(--r)':on&&v>=60?'var(--am)':'var(--t)'}
    g.classList.remove('highlight','warning','peak-gauge');
    if(on&&v>=80)g.classList.add('highlight');
    else if(on&&v>=60)g.classList.add('warning');
  });
  /* Smart emphasis: highest-load gauge gets extra border glow even below threshold */
  if(on){
    const maxVal=Math.max(...vals);const maxIdx=vals.indexOf(maxVal);
    if(maxVal>=10&&gauges[maxIdx]){gauges[maxIdx].classList.add('peak-gauge')}
  }
  /* Update status strip cells */
  const strip=document.querySelector('#pg-detail .det-strip');
  if(strip){
    const cells=strip.querySelectorAll('.ds-v');
    const health=on?Math.max(0,Math.round(100-(cpu*0.4+ram*0.35+disk*0.25))):0;
    function statusGrade(h){if(!on)return{text:'OFFLINE',cls:'offline'};if(h>=80)return{text:'ACTIVE',cls:'st-active'};if(h>=60)return{text:'STABLE',cls:'st-stable'};if(h>=40)return{text:'WARNING',cls:'st-warning'};return{text:'CRITICAL',cls:'st-critical'}}
    const grade=statusGrade(health);
    if(cells[0]){cells[0].className='ds-v '+(on?'online':'offline');cells[0].textContent=on?'ONLINE':'OFFLINE'}
    if(cells[1]){cells[1].className='ds-v '+grade.cls;cells[1].textContent=grade.text}
    if(cells[2]){cells[2].textContent=on?health+'%':'--';cells[2].style.color=on?(health>=80?'var(--g)':health>=60?'var(--cyan)':health>=40?'var(--am)':'var(--r)'):'var(--t4)'}
  }
  /* Update panel rows
     Index map (SYSTEM INFO 0-8 + RESOURCES 9-17):
       0 REGION / 1 GROUP / 2 OS / 3 UPTIME / 4 CPU MODEL / 5 CORES
       6 BANDWIDTH / 7 TRAFFIC / 8 MONTHLY
       9 CPU / 10 RAM / 11 SWAP / 12 DISK / 13 NET UP / 14 NET DOWN
       15 TOTAL UP / 16 TOTAL DOWN / 17 TCP/UDP */
  const rows=document.querySelectorAll('#pg-detail .det-row-v');
  if(rows.length>=18){
    rows[3].textContent=on?fUs(d.uptime):'--';
    rows[9].textContent=on?cpu+'%':'--';rows[9].style.color=on&&cpu>=80?'var(--r)':'';
    rows[10].textContent=on?fB(d.memory_used||0)+' / '+fB(d.memory_total||0):'--';rows[10].style.color=on&&ram>=80?'var(--r)':'';
    rows[11].textContent=on?fB(d.swap_used||0)+' / '+fB(d.swap_total||0):'--';
    rows[12].textContent=on?fB(d.disk_used||0)+' / '+fB(d.disk_total||0):'--';rows[12].style.color=on&&disk>=80?'var(--r)':'';
    rows[13].textContent=on?fS(d.network_tx||0):'--';
    rows[14].textContent=on?fS(d.network_rx||0):'--';
    rows[15].textContent=on?fB(d.network_total_up||0,1):'--';
    rows[16].textContent=on?fB(d.network_total_down||0,1):'--';
    rows[17].textContent=on?(d.tcp_conn_count||d.tcp||0)+' / '+(d.udp_conn_count||d.udp||0):'--';
  }
}

/* ── Enhanced Canvas Chart — tactical glow + peak + current value ── */
function cAlpha(c,a){
  if(c.startsWith('#')){var hex=c.slice(1);if(hex.length===3)hex=hex[0]+hex[0]+hex[1]+hex[1]+hex[2]+hex[2];return 'rgba('+parseInt(hex.slice(0,2),16)+','+parseInt(hex.slice(2,4),16)+','+parseInt(hex.slice(4,6),16)+','+a+')'}
  var m=c.match(/[\d.]+/g);if(m&&m.length>=3)return 'rgba('+m[0]+','+m[1]+','+m[2]+','+a+')';return c;
}
function dCh(canvasId,opts){
  const canvas=$(canvasId);if(!canvas)return;
  const ctx=canvas.getContext('2d');
  const dpr=window.devicePixelRatio||1;
  canvas.style.width='';canvas.style.height='';
  const cs=getComputedStyle(canvas);
  const w=parseFloat(cs.width)||180;
  const chH=parseFloat(cs.height)||180;
  canvas.width=Math.round(w*dpr);canvas.height=Math.round(chH*dpr);
  canvas.style.width=w+'px';canvas.style.height=chH+'px';
  ctx.scale(dpr,dpr);
  const h=chH,pad={t:10,r:16,b:30,l:45};
  let data=opts.data||[];
  let labels=opts.labels||[];
  let rawTimes=opts.rawTimes||[];
  if(!data.length)return;
  /* Downsample if too many points — LTTB-like: pick max in each bucket */
  const maxPts=Math.min(data.length,120);
  if(data.length>maxPts){
    const bSz=data.length/maxPts;const nd=[];const nl=[];const nr=[];
    for(let i=0;i<maxPts;i++){
      const s=Math.floor(i*bSz),e=Math.min(Math.floor((i+1)*bSz),data.length);
      let mI=s;for(let j=s+1;j<e;j++){if(data[j]>data[mI])mI=j}
      /* Use average for smoother look, but keep peak info */
      let sum=0;for(let j=s;j<e;j++)sum+=data[j];
      nd.push(sum/(e-s));
      const mid=Math.floor((s+e)/2);
      nl.push(labels[mid]||'');
      nr.push(rawTimes[mid]||0);
    }
    data=nd;labels=nl;rawTimes=nr;
  }
  /* Smart Y-axis: add breathing room so small fluctuations look calm */
  let max=opts.max;
  if(!max){
    const sorted=data.slice().filter(v=>v>0).sort((a,b)=>a-b);
    const dMax=Math.max(...data);
    const dMin=sorted[0]||0;
    const median=sorted[Math.floor(sorted.length/2)]||dMax;
    const p95=sorted[Math.floor(sorted.length*0.95)]||dMax;
    const range=p95-dMin;
    if(dMax<=0){max=10}
    else if(range<1){
      /* Nearly flat — show 0 to 2x or at least 5 */
      max=Math.max(dMax*2,5);
    }else{
      /* Use p95 as anchor, add full range as headroom above */
      max=p95+range;
      /* Ensure peak is visible */
      if(dMax>max)max=dMax*1.1;
    }
    /* Round to nice number */
    if(max>=100){max=Math.ceil(max/10)*10}
    else if(max>=10){max=Math.ceil(max/5)*5}
    else{max=Math.ceil(max)}
    if(max<=0)max=10;
  }
  const cw=w-pad.l-pad.r,ch=h-pad.t-pad.b;
  const color=opts.color||'#2563eb';
  /* Grid */
  ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(148,163,184,0.2)';ctx.lineWidth=0.5;
  for(let i=0;i<=4;i++){
    const y=pad.t+ch*(i/4);
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.moveTo(pad.l,y);ctx.lineTo(w-pad.r,y);ctx.stroke();
    ctx.fillStyle='#64748b';ctx.font='9px JetBrains Mono';ctx.textAlign='right';
    ctx.fillText(Math.round(max*(1-i/4)),pad.l-6,y+3);
  }
  /* Build path points — use real timestamps for x position if available */
  let pts;
  if(rawTimes.length===data.length&&rawTimes[0]&&rawTimes[rawTimes.length-1]){
    const tMin=rawTimes[0],tMax=rawTimes[rawTimes.length-1],tRange=tMax-tMin||1;
    pts=data.map((v,i)=>({x:pad.l+((rawTimes[i]-tMin)/tRange)*cw,y:pad.t+ch*(1-Math.min(v,max)/max)}));
  }else{
    pts=data.map((v,i)=>({x:pad.l+(i/(data.length-1||1))*cw,y:pad.t+ch*(1-Math.min(v,max)/max)}));
  }
  /* X-axis time labels */
  if(rawTimes.length>1&&rawTimes[0]&&rawTimes[rawTimes.length-1]){
    ctx.fillStyle='#94a3b8';ctx.font='8px JetBrains Mono';ctx.textAlign='center';
    const tickCount=Math.min(5,data.length);
    const tMin=rawTimes[0],tMax=rawTimes[rawTimes.length-1],tRange=tMax-tMin||1;
    /* Detect cross-day */
    let needDate=false;
    const d1=new Date(tMin);const d2=new Date(tMax);
    if(d1.getDate()!==d2.getDate()||d1.getMonth()!==d2.getMonth())needDate=true;
    /* Generate evenly spaced time ticks */
    for(let i=0;i<tickCount;i++){
      const t=tMin+i*tRange/(tickCount-1);
      const x=pad.l+(i/(tickCount-1))*cw;
      const d=new Date(t);
      const hh=String(d.getHours()).padStart(2,'0');
      const mm=String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2,'0');
      let display=hh+':'+mm;
      if(needDate){
        const M=String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0');
        const D=String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,'0');
        display=M+'/'+D+' '+display;
      }
      if(i===0){ctx.textAlign='left';ctx.fillText(display,Math.max(x,pad.l),h-4);ctx.textAlign='center'}
      else if(i===tickCount-1){ctx.textAlign='right';ctx.fillText(display,Math.min(x,w-pad.r),h-4);ctx.textAlign='center'}
      else{ctx.fillText(display,x,h-4)}
    }
  }
  /* Smooth bezier helper */
  function drawSmooth(points){
    if(points.length<2)return;
    ctx.moveTo(points[0].x,points[0].y);
    if(points.length===2){ctx.lineTo(points[1].x,points[1].y);return}
    /* Catmull-Rom → cubic bezier for smooth curve */
    for(let i=0;i<points.length-1;i++){
      const p0=points[Math.max(0,i-1)];
      const p1=points[i];
      const p2=points[i+1];
      const p3=points[Math.min(points.length-1,i+2)];
      const tension=0.25;
      const cp1x=p1.x+(p2.x-p0.x)*tension;
      const cp1y=p1.y+(p2.y-p0.y)*tension;
      const cp2x=p2.x-(p3.x-p1.x)*tension;
      const cp2y=p2.y-(p3.y-p1.y)*tension;
      ctx.bezierCurveTo(cp1x,cp1y,cp2x,cp2y,p2.x,p2.y);
    }
  }
  /* Glow layer */
  ctx.save();
  ctx.shadowColor=color;ctx.shadowBlur=14;ctx.shadowOffsetY=0;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.strokeStyle=cAlpha(color,0.25);ctx.lineWidth=5;ctx.lineJoin='round';ctx.lineCap='round';
  drawSmooth(pts);
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();
  /* Main line */
  ctx.save();
  ctx.shadowColor=color;ctx.shadowBlur=6;ctx.shadowOffsetY=1;
  ctx.beginPath();ctx.strokeStyle=color;ctx.lineWidth=2;ctx.lineJoin='round';ctx.lineCap='round';
  drawSmooth(pts);
  ctx.stroke();
  ctx.restore();
  /* Fill gradient under curve */
  ctx.beginPath();
  drawSmooth(pts);
  ctx.lineTo(pts[pts.length-1].x,pad.t+ch);ctx.lineTo(pts[0].x,pad.t+ch);ctx.closePath();
  const grad=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,pad.t,0,pad.t+ch);
  grad.addColorStop(0,cAlpha(color,0.15));grad.addColorStop(0.6,cAlpha(color,0.03));grad.addColorStop(1,cAlpha(color,0.01));
  ctx.fillStyle=grad;ctx.fill();
  /* Peak dot with glow ring — use original data for accurate peak */
  const origData=opts.data||[];
  const peakVal=Math.max(...origData);const peakIdx=origData.indexOf(peakVal);
  if(peakIdx>=0&&pts.length>1){
    /* Map peakIdx back to downsampled position */
    const ratio=peakIdx/(origData.length-1||1);
    const px=pad.l+ratio*cw;const py=pad.t+ch*(1-Math.min(peakVal,max)/max);
    ctx.save();ctx.shadowColor=color;ctx.shadowBlur=10;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(px,py,5,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle=cAlpha(color,0.19);ctx.fill();
    ctx.restore();
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(px,py,3.5,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle=color;ctx.fill();
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(px,py,1.5,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle='#fff';ctx.fill();
    ctx.font='bold 9px Outfit';ctx.fillStyle=color;ctx.textAlign='center';
    ctx.fillText(opts.max?peakVal.toFixed(0):peakVal.toFixed(1),px,py-10);
  }
  /* Current value dot (last point) */
  if(pts.length>1){
    const lp=pts[pts.length-1];const lv=origData[origData.length-1]||data[data.length-1];
    ctx.save();ctx.shadowColor=color;ctx.shadowBlur=8;
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(lp.x,lp.y,4,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle=color;ctx.fill();
    ctx.restore();
    ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(lp.x,lp.y,2,0,Math.PI*2);ctx.fillStyle='#fff';ctx.fill();
    ctx.font='bold 10px Outfit';ctx.fillStyle=color;ctx.textAlign='left';
    ctx.fillText(opts.max?lv.toFixed(0):lv.toFixed(1),lp.x+8,lp.y+3);
    const wrap=canvas.closest('.chart-wrap');
    if(wrap){
      let cur=wrap.querySelector('.chart-cur');
      if(!cur){cur=document.createElement('div');cur.className='chart-cur';wrap.appendChild(cur)}
      cur.innerHTML=(opts.max?lv.toFixed(0):lv.toFixed(1))+'<span>'+(opts.label||'%')+'</span>';
      let pulse=wrap.querySelector('.chart-pulse');
      if(!pulse){pulse=document.createElement('div');pulse.className='chart-pulse';wrap.appendChild(pulse)}
      const canvasRect=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();const wrapRect=wrap.getBoundingClientRect();
      pulse.style.left=(lp.x+canvas.offsetLeft)+'px';
      pulse.style.top=(lp.y+(canvasRect.top-wrapRect.top))+'px';
      pulse.style.borderColor=color;
    }
  }
  // Save chart meta for tooltip
  var dark=document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme')==='dark';
  canvas._chMeta={pts:pts,data:data,rawTimes:rawTimes,max:max,pad:pad,color:color,w:w,h:h,label:opts.label||'',dpr:dpr,cw:cw,ch:ch,dark:dark};
  if(!canvas._chBound){
    canvas._chBound=true;
    canvas.style.cursor='crosshair';
    var twrap=canvas.parentElement;
    if(twrap)twrap.style.position='relative';
    var tline=document.createElement('div');
    tline.style.cssText='position:absolute;top:0;bottom:0;width:1px;pointer-events:none;display:none;z-index:5;border-left:1px dashed rgba(100,116,139,0.35)';
    var tdot=document.createElement('div');
    tdot.style.cssText='position:absolute;width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;pointer-events:none;display:none;z-index:6;transform:translate(-50%,-50%);box-shadow:0 0 6px currentColor';
    var ttip=document.createElement('div');
    ttip.style.cssText='position:absolute;pointer-events:none;display:none;z-index:7;padding:6px 10px;border-radius:6px;font-size:12px;line-height:1.5;white-space:nowrap;border:1px solid rgba(148,163,184,0.25);box-shadow:0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.1)';
    twrap.appendChild(tline);twrap.appendChild(tdot);twrap.appendChild(ttip);
    canvas._tipEls={line:tline,dot:tdot,tip:ttip};
    canvas.addEventListener('mousemove',function(e){
      var m=canvas._chMeta;if(!m||!m.pts.length)return;
      var el=canvas._tipEls;
      var cr=canvas.getBoundingClientRect();
      var offX=canvas.offsetLeft,offY=canvas.offsetTop;
      var mx=e.clientX-cr.left;
      var ratioX=mx/cr.width;
      var chartX=ratioX*m.w;
      var best=0,bestD=Infinity;
      for(var i=0;i<m.pts.length;i++){var dx=Math.abs(m.pts[i].x-chartX);if(dx<bestD){bestD=dx;best=i}}
      var p=m.pts[best],v=m.data[best],t=m.rawTimes[best];
      var pxX=offX+(p.x/m.w)*cr.width;
      var pxY=offY+(p.y/m.h)*cr.height;
      el.line.style.display='block';el.line.style.left=pxX+'px';
      el.line.style.borderColor=m.dark?'rgba(0,212,240,0.3)':'rgba(100,116,139,0.35)';
      el.dot.style.display='block';el.dot.style.left=pxX+'px';el.dot.style.top=pxY+'px';
      el.dot.style.background=m.color;el.dot.style.color=m.color;
      var valTxt=v!=null?v.toFixed(1)+' '+(m.label||''):'--';
      var timeTxt='';
      if(t){var d=new Date(t);timeTxt=String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')+'/'+String(d.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')+' '+String(d.getHours()).padStart(2,'0')+':'+String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2,'0')}
      el.tip.style.display='block';
      el.tip.style.background=m.dark?'rgba(14,26,45,0.92)':'rgba(255,255,255,0.92)';
      el.tip.style.borderColor=m.dark?'rgba(0,212,240,0.2)':'rgba(148,163,184,0.25)';
      el.tip.innerHTML='<div style="font-family:Outfit;font-weight:700;color:'+m.color+'">'+valTxt+'</div><div style="font-family:JetBrains Mono;font-size:10px;color:'+(m.dark?'#7d9ab5':'#64748b')+'">'+timeTxt+'</div>';
      var tx=pxX+12,ty=pxY-50;
      var tipW=el.tip.offsetWidth;
      if(tx+tipW>twrap.offsetWidth-8)tx=pxX-tipW-12;
      if(ty<0)ty=pxY+12;
      el.tip.style.left=tx+'px';el.tip.style.top=ty+'px';
    });
    canvas.addEventListener('mouseleave',function(){
      var el=canvas._tipEls;if(!el)return;
      el.line.style.display='none';el.dot.style.display='none';el.tip.style.display='none';
    });
  }
}

/* ── Stability ── */
async function loadStabilityData(){
  STAB.loading=true;
  await fetchStabTasks();
  await fetchStability(STAB.hours);
  STAB.loading=false;
}
async function fetchStabTasks(){
  try{
    if(!S.nodes.length)return;
    const uuid=S.nodes[0].uuid;
    const r=await fetch(`/api/records/ping?uuid=${uuid}&hours=1`);const j=await r.json();const d=j.data||j;
    if(d.tasks&&d.tasks.length){STAB.tasks=d.tasks;STAB._tasksFromApi=true;renderStabTasks()}
  }catch(e){}
}
async function fetchStability(hours){
  /* Warn on large time ranges */
  if(hours>=720){if(!confirm('30天数据量较大，加载可能较慢。确认加载？'))return}
  try{
    STAB.loading=true;
    const c=$('stabContent');
    if(c)c.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:#6a8098">加载中... 逐节点查询以节省内存</div>';

    /* Per-node sequential fetch — prevents server OOM */
    const allRecords=[];
    const nodes=S.nodes||[];
    for(let i=0;i<nodes.length;i++){
      const uuid=nodes[i].uuid;
      try{
        const r=await fetch('/api/records/ping?uuid='+uuid+'&hours='+hours);
        const j=await r.json();
        const dd=j.data||j;
        const recs=dd.records||[];
        /* Tag each record with node uuid if missing */
        for(let k=0;k<recs.length;k++){
          if(!recs[k].client&&!recs[k].uuid&&!recs[k].node_uuid)recs[k].client=uuid;
        }
        allRecords.push.apply(allRecords,recs);
        /* Extract tasks from first node that has them */
        if(!STAB._tasksFromApi&&dd.tasks&&dd.tasks.length){
          STAB.tasks=dd.tasks;STAB._tasksFromApi=true;
        }
        /* Progress update */
        if(c)c.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:#6a8098">加载中... '+(i+1)+'/'+nodes.length+'</div>';
      }catch(e){/* skip failed node */}
    }
    STAB.data={records:allRecords};
    STAB.loading=false;
    if(STAB._tasksFromApi)renderStabTasks();
    renderStability();
  }catch(e){
    STAB.loading=false;
    const c=$('stabContent');if(c)c.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:var(--r)">Failed to load stability data</div>';
  }
}
function extractTasksFromData(data){
  if(!data)return;
  // RPC2 ping results have basic_info array but no task names per record
  // Tasks from /api/records/ping?uuid=X are more reliable, so only fallback here
  if(data.basic_info&&data.basic_info.length){
    const ts=new Map();
    data.basic_info.forEach(b=>{if(b.client&&!ts.has(b.client))ts.set(b.client,b.client.slice(0,8))});
  }
  renderStabTasks();
}
function renderStabTasks(){
  const c=$('stabTasks');if(!c)return;
  c.innerHTML=`<button class="pill${STAB.taskId===null?' a':''}" data-tid="ALL">ALL</button>`+
    STAB.tasks.map(t=>`<button class="pill${STAB.taskId===t.id?' a':''}" data-tid="${t.id}">${esc(t.name)}</button>`).join('');
  c.querySelectorAll('.pill').forEach(b=>{
    b.onclick=()=>{STAB.taskId=b.dataset.tid==='ALL'?null:+b.dataset.tid;renderStability();renderStabTasks()}
  });
}
function stabAggByDay(records){
  if(!records)return{};
  /* Build per-node per-day aggregation — optimized for large datasets */
  const byNode={};
  for(let i=0,len=records.length;i<len;i++){
    const r=records[i];
    if(STAB.taskId!==null&&r.task_id!==STAB.taskId)continue;
    const uuid=r.client||r.uuid||r.node_uuid;if(!uuid)continue;
    const t=r.time||r.created_at||r.timestamp;if(!t)continue;
    /* Extract YYYY-MM-DD from ISO string directly, avoid new Date() */
