    const day=typeof t==='string'&&t.length>=10?t.slice(0,10):new Date(t).toISOString().slice(0,10);
    let n=byNode[uuid];
    if(!n){n={days:{},total:0,loss:0};byNode[uuid]=n}
    let d=n.days[day];
    if(!d){d={total:0,loss:0};n.days[day]=d}
    d.total++;n.total++;
    if(r.value<0){d.loss++;n.loss++}
  }
  return byNode;
}
function renderStability(){
  const c=$('stabContent');if(!c||!STAB.data)return;
  const records=STAB.data.records||[];
  const agg=stabAggByDay(records);

  /* Generate date range for heatmap columns */
  const days=[];
  const now=new Date();
  const numDays=STAB.hours<=24?1:STAB.hours<=168?7:30;
  for(let i=numDays-1;i>=0;i--){
    const d=new Date(now);d.setDate(d.getDate()-i);
    days.push(d.toISOString().slice(0,10));
  }

  /* Overview stats */
  let totalNodes=Object.keys(agg).length,perfect=0;
  Object.values(agg).forEach(v=>{
    const pct=v.total?((v.total-v.loss)/v.total*100):100;
    if(pct>=99.99)perfect++;
  });
  const fleetUp=totalNodes?Object.values(agg).reduce((s,v)=>s+(v.total?(v.total-v.loss)/v.total*100:100),0)/totalNodes:0;
  const targetName=STAB.taskId?STAB.tasks.find(t=>t.id===STAB.taskId)?.name||'--':'ALL';

  let html=`<div class="stab-ov">
    <div class="stab-ov-card"><div class="det-label">FLEET UPTIME</div><div class="det-val" style="color:var(--g)">${fleetUp.toFixed(2)}%</div></div>
    <div class="stab-ov-card"><div class="det-label">TOTAL NODES</div><div class="det-val">${totalNodes}</div></div>
    <div class="stab-ov-card"><div class="det-label">PERFECT</div><div class="det-val" style="color:var(--g)">${perfect}</div></div>
    <div class="stab-ov-card"><div class="det-label">CURRENT TARGET</div><div class="det-val">${esc(targetName)}</div></div>
  </div>`;

  /* Date header */
  if(numDays>1){
    html+=`<div class="stab-date-row"><div class="stab-row-name"></div><div class="stab-date-labels">`;
    days.forEach((d,i)=>{
      const show=i===0||i===days.length-1||i%7===0;
      html+=`<div class="stab-date-lbl">${show?d.slice(5).replace('-','/'):'  '}</div>`;
    });
    html+=`</div><div style="width:65px"></div></div>`;
  }

  /* Heatmap matrix */
  html+=`<div class="stab-matrix">`;
  const sorted=S.nodes.filter(n=>agg[n.uuid]).map(n=>{
    const a=agg[n.uuid];const pct=a.total?((a.total-a.loss)/a.total*100):100;
    return{node:n,pct,agg:a};
  });
  if(STAB.sort==='uptime')sorted.sort((a,b)=>a.pct-b.pct);
  else if(STAB.sort==='loss')sorted.sort((a,b)=>b.agg.loss-a.agg.loss);
  else sorted.sort((a,b)=>(a.node.name||'').localeCompare(b.node.name||''));

  sorted.forEach(({node,pct,agg:a})=>{
    const pctColor=pct>=99.9?'var(--g)':pct>=95?'var(--am)':'var(--r)';
    html+=`<div class="stab-row"><div class="stab-row-name">${esc(node.name||node.uuid)}</div><div class="stab-heatmap">`;
    days.forEach(day=>{
      const dd=a.days[day];
      if(!dd){html+=`<div class="stab-cell empty"></div>`;return}
      const dayPct=dd.total?((dd.total-dd.loss)/dd.total*100):100;
      const cls=dayPct>=99.99?'c100':dayPct>=99?'c99':dayPct>=95?'c95':dayPct>=90?'c90':'c0';
      const lostMin=dd.loss>0?Math.round(dd.loss*5)+'min':'0';
      html+=`<div class="stab-cell ${cls}" title="${day}: ${dayPct.toFixed(1)}%"><div class="stab-tip">${day.slice(5)}<br>${dayPct.toFixed(1)}%${dd.loss?' · '+lostMin+' down':''}</div></div>`;
    });
    html+=`</div><div class="stab-row-pct" style="color:${pctColor}">${pct.toFixed(2)}%</div></div>`;
  });
  html+=`</div>`;
  c.innerHTML=html;

  /* Time & sort buttons */
  const tr=$('stabTime');
  if(tr){
    const stabMaxH=S.pingRetention||720;
    const stabSteps=genTimeSteps(stabMaxH);
    tr.innerHTML=stabSteps.map(h=>`<button class="${h===STAB.hours?'a':''}" data-h="${h}">${fmtH(h)}</button>`).join('')+
      '&nbsp;&nbsp;'+['name','uptime','loss'].map(s=>`<button class="${s===STAB.sort?'a':''}" data-s="${s}">${s.toUpperCase()}</button>`).join('');
    tr.querySelectorAll('button[data-h]').forEach(b=>{
      b.onclick=()=>{STAB.hours=+b.dataset.h;fetchStability(STAB.hours)}
    });
    tr.querySelectorAll('button[data-s]').forEach(b=>{
      b.onclick=()=>{STAB.sort=b.dataset.s;renderStability()}
    });
  }
}

/* ── Routing ── */
function showP(page){if(page!=='stability'&&STAB.data){STAB.data=null};
  document.querySelectorAll('.page').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('active'));
  const pg=$('pg-'+page);if(pg)pg.classList.add('active');
  document.querySelectorAll('.tb-tab').forEach(t=>{
    t.classList.toggle('a',t.dataset.page===page);
  });
}
function hRoute(){
  const path=location.pathname;
  if(path.startsWith('/detail/')){
    const uuid=path.split('/detail/')[1];
    if(uuid){
      S.detailUUID=uuid;S.detailNode=S.nodes.find(n=>n.uuid===uuid);
      showP('detail');
      if(S.detailNode)rDetInfo(S.detailNode,uuid);
    }
  }else if(path==='/stability'){
    showP('stability');loadStabilityData();
  }else if(path==='/billing'){
    showP('billing');if(!S._ratesFetched){fetchRates().then(function(){rBilling()}).catch(function(){rBilling()})}else{rBilling()}
  }else if(path==='/worldmap'){
    S._wmInited=false;showP('worldmap');initWorldMap();
  }else{
    showP('dashboard');
  }
}
function nav(path){
  history.pushState(null,null,path);hRoute();
}
window.nav=nav;
window.openDet=function(uuid){
  S.detailUUID=uuid;S.detailNode=S.nodes.find(n=>n.uuid===uuid);
  S.detailTab='load';S.detailHours=6;S.detailPingHours=6;S.detailWsData=[];
  nav('/detail/'+uuid);
};
window.addEventListener('popstate',hRoute);

/* ── Tab nav ── */
document.querySelectorAll('.tb-tab').forEach(b=>{
  b.onclick=()=>{
    const p=b.dataset.page;
    if(p==='dashboard')nav('/');
    else if(p==='stability')nav('/stability');
    else if(p==='worldmap')nav('/worldmap');
    else if(p==='billing')nav('/billing');
    else if(p==='detail')window.location.href='/nexus.html';
  }
});


/* ── Billing Functions ── */

/* ── Parse node labels for bandwidth/traffic info ── */
/* Labels format: '2Gbps<green>;3T<blue>' or '1Gbps;3T' */
function parseLabels(node){
  var result={bandwidth:null,traffic:null,allLabels:[]};
  var raw=node.labels||node.tags||'';
  if(!raw||typeof raw!=='string')return result;
  var parts=raw.split(';');
  parts.forEach(function(p){
    p=p.trim();if(!p)return;
    /* Strip color tag like <green>, <blue> etc */
    var text=p.replace(/<[^>]+>/g,'').trim();
    var color=(p.match(/<([^>]+)>/)||[])[1]||'';
    result.allLabels.push({text:text,color:color});
    /* Detect bandwidth: contains Gbps, Mbps, gbps, mbps */
    if(/\d+\.?\d*\s*[gGmM]bps/i.test(text)){
      result.bandwidth=text;
    }
    /* Detect traffic: contains T, G, TB, GB (but not bps) */
    else if(/^\d+\.?\d*\s*[TtGg][Bb]?$/i.test(text)){
      result.traffic=text;
    }
  });
  return result;
}

function fBilling(n){
  if(!n.price||n.price===0)return{str:'',monthly:0,currency:''};
  if(n.price===-1)return{str:'免费',monthly:0,currency:''};
  var cur=n.currency||'$';
  var p=n.price;
  var cDays=parseInt(n.billing_cycle)||30;
  var cycleStr='';var months=1;
  if(cDays<=31){cycleStr='/月';months=1}
  else if(cDays<=93){cycleStr='/季';months=3}
  else if(cDays<=186){cycleStr='/半年';months=6}
  else if(cDays<=366){cycleStr='/年';months=12}
  else if(cDays<=1096){cycleStr='/三年';months=36}
  else{var yrs=Math.round(cDays/365);cycleStr='/'+yrs+'年';months=yrs*12}
  var monthly=p/months;
  return{str:cur+p+cycleStr,monthly:monthly,currency:cur};
}

S._billView=S._billView||'group';
function setBillView(v){S._billView=v;document.querySelectorAll('.bf-vbtn').forEach(function(b){b.classList.toggle('a',b.getAttribute('data-view')===v)});rBilling()}
document.querySelectorAll('.bf-vbtn').forEach(function(b){b.addEventListener('click',function(){setBillView(this.getAttribute('data-view'))})});


/* ═══ Currency Exchange System ═══ */
S._displayCurrency='USD';
S._rates=null;
S._rateBase='USD';
S._ratesFetched=false;
S._currencySymbols={USD:'$',CNY:'¥',EUR:'€',JPY:'¥',GBP:'£'};

async function fetchRates(){
  if(S._ratesFetched)return;
  var fallback={USD:1,CNY:7.25,EUR:0.92,JPY:150.5,GBP:0.79,AUD:1.55,CAD:1.36,HKD:7.82,TWD:32.5,SGD:1.34,KRW:1380};
  try{
    var ctrl=new AbortController();
    var tid=setTimeout(function(){ctrl.abort()},5000);
    var r=await fetch('https://open.er-api.com/v6/latest/USD',{signal:ctrl.signal});
    clearTimeout(tid);
    var j=await r.json();
    if(j.result==='success'&&j.rates){S._rates=j.rates;S._rateBase='USD';S._ratesFetched=true;/* rates loaded */;return}
  }catch(e){console.warn('Rate API failed:',e.message)}
  S._rates=fallback;S._rateBase='USD';S._ratesFetched=true;/* rates loaded */;
}

function convertCurrency(amount,fromSymbol,toCur){
  if(!S._rates||toCur==='original')return null;
  /* Map currency symbol to code */
  var fromCode=null;
  var symbolMap={'$':'USD','¥':'CNY','€':'EUR','£':'GBP','₩':'KRW','₽':'RUB','₹':'INR','฿':'THB','A$':'AUD','C$':'CAD','HK$':'HKD','NT$':'TWD','S$':'SGD','R$':'BRL'};
  /* Try direct symbol match */
  fromCode=symbolMap[fromSymbol];
  /* If ¥ and target is CNY, assume source is JPY and vice versa */
  if(fromSymbol==='¥'){
    /* Heuristic: if amount > 100 likely JPY, else CNY */
    fromCode=amount>100?'JPY':'CNY';
  }
  if(!fromCode)fromCode='USD';
  if(fromCode===toCur)return{amount:amount,symbol:S._currencySymbols[toCur]||toCur};
  var fromRate=S._rates[fromCode]||1;
  var toRate=S._rates[toCur]||1;
  var converted=amount/fromRate*toRate;
  return{amount:converted,symbol:S._currencySymbols[toCur]||toCur};
}

function setCurrency(cur){
  S._displayCurrency=cur;
  document.querySelectorAll('.bill-cur-btn').forEach(function(b){b.classList.toggle('a',b.getAttribute('data-cur')===cur)});
  if(cur!=='original'&&!S._ratesFetched){
    var sumEl=$('billSummary');
    if(sumEl)sumEl.innerHTML='<div class="bf-ov-card" style="grid-column:1/-1;text-align:center;padding:28px"><div class="bf-ov-val" style="color:var(--t4);font-size:16px">获取汇率中...</div></div>';
    fetchRates().then(function(){rBilling()}).catch(function(){rBilling()});
  }else{rBilling()}
}
window.setCurrency=setCurrency;

function fmtConverted(amount,fromSymbol){
  if(S._displayCurrency==='original')return fromSymbol+amount.toFixed(2);
  var c=convertCurrency(amount,fromSymbol,S._displayCurrency);
  if(!c)return fromSymbol+amount.toFixed(2);
  return c.symbol+c.amount.toFixed(2);
}

function rBilling(){
  var sumEl=$('billSummary');var contentEl=$('billContent');
  if(!sumEl||!contentEl)return;
  var totals={};var nodeRows=[];var freeCount=0;var groupData={};
  S.nodes.forEach(function(n){
    if(n.hidden)return;
    var b=fBilling(n);
    var on=S.onlineSet.has(n.uuid);
    var g=n.group||'未分组';
    if(b.monthly>0&&b.currency){
      if(!totals[b.currency])totals[b.currency]=0;
      totals[b.currency]+=b.monthly;
    }
    if(b.str==='免费')freeCount++;
    var rv=0,rd=0;
    if(n.expired_at&&b.monthly>0&&b.currency){
      var ed=new Date(n.expired_at);var nw=new Date();
      rd=Math.max(0,Math.ceil((ed-nw)/(86400000)));
      if(rd>3650)rd=0;
      var cdd=parseInt(n.billing_cycle)||30;
      rv=cdd>0?(rd/cdd)*n.price:0;
      if(rv>b.monthly*120)rv=0;
    }
    var row={node:n,billing:b,online:on,group:g,remainVal:rv,remainDays:rd};
    nodeRows.push(row);
    if(!groupData[g])groupData[g]={rows:[],totals:{},remainTotals:{}};
    groupData[g].rows.push(row);
    if(b.monthly>0&&b.currency){
      if(!groupData[g].totals[b.currency])groupData[g].totals[b.currency]=0;
      groupData[g].totals[b.currency]+=b.monthly;
    }
    if(rv>0&&b.currency){
      if(!groupData[g].remainTotals[b.currency])groupData[g].remainTotals[b.currency]=0;
      groupData[g].remainTotals[b.currency]+=rv;
    }
  });

  var dc=S._displayCurrency;
  var totalEntries=Object.entries(totals);

  /* Resource Overview (3 cards) */
  var mTotal=0,yTotal=0,rTotal=0;
  var sym=dc!=='original'&&S._currencySymbols[dc]?S._currencySymbols[dc]:'$';
  var remainTotals={};
  nodeRows.forEach(function(r){if(r.remainVal>0&&r.billing.currency){var c=r.billing.currency;if(!remainTotals[c])remainTotals[c]=0;remainTotals[c]+=r.remainVal;}});
  if(dc!=='original'&&S._rates){
    totalEntries.forEach(function(e){var c=convertCurrency(e[1],e[0],dc);mTotal+=c?c.amount:e[1]});
    Object.entries(remainTotals).forEach(function(e){var c=convertCurrency(e[1],e[0],dc);rTotal+=c?c.amount:e[1]});
    sym=S._currencySymbols[dc]||dc;
  }else{
    totalEntries.forEach(function(e){mTotal+=e[1]});
    Object.entries(remainTotals).forEach(function(e){rTotal+=e[1]});
    if(totalEntries.length===1)sym=totalEntries[0][0];
  }
  yTotal=mTotal*12;
  var sh='';
  sh+='<div class="bf-ov-card" style="box-shadow:0 0 28px rgba(var(--cyan-rgb),0.12)"><div class="bf-ov-val cyan">'+sym+mTotal.toFixed(2)+'</div><div class="bf-ov-label">CURRENT LOAD</div><div class="bf-ov-sub">MONTHLY RESOURCE COST</div></div>';
  sh+='<div class="bf-ov-card" style="box-shadow:0 0 28px rgba(var(--cyan-rgb),0.10)"><div class="bf-ov-val cyan">'+sym+yTotal.toFixed(2)+'</div><div class="bf-ov-label">PROJECTED</div><div class="bf-ov-sub">ANNUAL RESOURCE LOAD</div></div>';
  sh+='<div class="bf-ov-card" style="box-shadow:0 0 28px rgba(var(--gr),0.10)"><div class="bf-ov-val green">'+sym+rTotal.toFixed(2)+'</div><div class="bf-ov-label">RESERVE</div><div class="bf-ov-sub">REMAINING BALANCE</div></div>';
  sumEl.innerHTML=sh;

  /* Cost Flow (group bars) */
  var flowEl=$('bfFlowBars');var flowTotEl=$('bfFlowTotal');
  if(flowEl){
    var groupNames=Object.keys(groupData).sort(function(a,b){
      var at=0,bt=0;Object.values(groupData[a].totals).forEach(function(v){at+=v});Object.values(groupData[b].totals).forEach(function(v){bt+=v});return bt-at;
    });
    var maxGroupCost=0;
    groupNames.forEach(function(gn){var gc=0;Object.values(groupData[gn].totals).forEach(function(v){gc+=v});if(gc>maxGroupCost)maxGroupCost=gc;});
    var colors=['cyan','blue','green','cyan','blue','green'];
    var fh='';
    groupNames.forEach(function(gn,idx){
      var gc=0;Object.values(groupData[gn].totals).forEach(function(v){gc+=v});
      if(gc<=0)return;
      var converted=gc;
      if(dc!=='original'&&S._rates){
        var cc=0;Object.entries(groupData[gn].totals).forEach(function(e){var cv=convertCurrency(e[1],e[0],dc);cc+=cv?cv.amount:e[1]});converted=cc;
      }
      var w=maxGroupCost>0?Math.max(6,Math.round((gc/maxGroupCost)*100)):6;
      var clr=colors[idx%colors.length];
      fh+='<div class="bf-flow-row"><div class="bf-flow-meta"><div>'+esc(gn)+'<span class="bf-flow-note"> \u00b7 '+groupData[gn].rows.length+' NODES</span></div><span class="bf-flow-val">'+sym+converted.toFixed(2)+'</span></div><div class="bf-flow-track"><div class="bf-flow-fill '+clr+'" style="width:'+w+'%"></div></div></div>';
    });
    flowEl.innerHTML=fh;
  }
  if(flowTotEl)flowTotEl.textContent=sym+mTotal.toFixed(2);

  /* Expiry Radar */
  var radarEl=$('bfRadarCounts');
  if(radarEl){
    var crit=0,warn=0,safe=0;
    nodeRows.forEach(function(r){
      if(!r.node.expired_at||r.billing.monthly<=0)return;
      if(r.remainDays<=7)crit++;
      else if(r.remainDays<=30)warn++;
      else safe++;
    });
    radarEl.innerHTML='<div class="bf-rc-item"><div class="bf-rc-label"><span class="bf-rc-dot rose"></span>CRITICAL</div><div class="bf-rc-val rose">'+crit+'</div></div>'
      +'<div class="bf-rc-item"><div class="bf-rc-label"><span class="bf-rc-dot amber"></span>WARNING</div><div class="bf-rc-val amber">'+warn+'</div></div>'
      +'<div class="bf-rc-item"><div class="bf-rc-label"><span class="bf-rc-dot green"></span>SAFE</div><div class="bf-rc-val green">'+safe+'</div></div>';
  }

  /* Due Queue */
  var dueEl=$('bfDueList');var dueTotEl=$('bfDueTotal');
  var now=new Date();var dueNodes=[];
  nodeRows.forEach(function(r){
    if(!r.node.expired_at)return;
    var exp=new Date(r.node.expired_at);
    var days=Math.ceil((exp-now)/(86400000));
    if(days>=0&&days<=30)dueNodes.push({name:r.node.name||r.node.uuid,uuid:r.node.uuid,days:days,billing:r.billing});
  });
  dueNodes.sort(function(a,b){return a.days-b.days});
  if(dueEl){
    if(dueNodes.length===0){
      dueEl.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:var(--t4);font-family:var(--fm);font-size:11px;letter-spacing:2px">NO DUE THIS MONTH</div>';
    }else{
      var dh='';
      dueNodes.forEach(function(d){
        var cls=d.days<=3?'urgent':d.days<=7?'soon':'ok';
        var label=d.days===0?'TODAY':d.days+' DAYS';
        var cost=d.billing.monthly>0?fmtConverted(d.billing.monthly,d.billing.currency):'--';
        dh+='<div class="bf-due-item" onclick="openDet(\''+d.uuid+'\')"><div><div class="bf-due-name">'+esc(d.name)+'</div><div class="bf-due-days '+cls+'">'+label+'</div></div><div class="bf-due-price">'+cost+'</div></div>';
      });
      dueEl.innerHTML=dh;
    }
  }
  if(dueTotEl){
    var dueTot=0;
    dueNodes.forEach(function(d){
      if(d.billing.monthly>0){
        if(dc!=='original'&&S._rates){var cv=convertCurrency(d.billing.monthly,d.billing.currency,dc);dueTot+=cv?cv.amount:d.billing.monthly;}
        else dueTot+=d.billing.monthly;
      }
    });
    dueTotEl.textContent=dueNodes.length>0?sym+dueTot.toFixed(2):'--';
  }

  /* Node Cost Stream */
  if(S._billView==='group'){rBillGroup(groupData)}
  else{rBillFlat(nodeRows)}

  renderCalendar();
}

function nodeRiskInfo(r){
  var days=r.remainDays;var b=r.billing;
  if(!r.node.expired_at||b.monthly<=0)return{risk:'NOMINAL',cls:'nominal',clr:'cyan'};
  if(days<=7)return{risk:'CRITICAL',cls:'critical',clr:'rose'};
  if(days<=30)return{risk:'WARNING',cls:'warning',clr:'amber'};
  return{risk:'SAFE',cls:'safe',clr:'green'};
}

function nodeCardHtml(r){
  var n=r.node;var b=r.billing;var ri=nodeRiskInfo(r);
  var monthlyDisp=b.monthly>0?fmtConverted(b.monthly,b.currency):(b.str==='\u514d\u8d39'?'\u514d\u8d39':'--');
  var remainDisp=r.remainVal>0?fmtConverted(r.remainVal,b.currency):'--';
  var daysLabel=r.remainDays>0?r.remainDays+'d':'--';
  var reserveW=10;
  if(b.monthly>0&&r.remainVal>0){reserveW=Math.min(100,Math.max(4,Math.round((r.remainVal/(b.monthly*12))*100)));}
  var expiryW=4;
  if(r.node.expired_at&&b.monthly>0){
    if(r.remainDays<=7)expiryW=92;
    else if(r.remainDays<=30)expiryW=65;
    else if(r.remainDays<=90)expiryW=40;
    else if(r.remainDays<=365)expiryW=20;
    else expiryW=8;
  }
  var daysNum=r.remainDays>0?String(r.remainDays):'\u221e';
  var h='<div class="bf-ncard" onclick="openDet(\''+n.uuid+'\')">';
  h+='<div class="bf-ncard-head"><div><div class="bf-ncard-name">'+esc(n.name||n.uuid)+'</div><div class="bf-ncard-unit">RESOURCE UNIT</div></div><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px"><button class="bill-export-btn" data-uuid="'+n.uuid+'" title="导出海报">⤓</button><span class="bf-pill '+ri.cls+'">'+ri.risk+'</span></div></div>';
  h+='<div class="bf-ncard-body"><div class="bf-ring-mini '+ri.clr+'"><div class="bf-ring-mini-inner">'+daysNum+'</div></div><div><div class="bf-ncard-cost '+ri.clr+'">'+monthlyDisp+'</div><div class="bf-ncard-costlbl">MONTHLY COST</div></div></div>';
  h+='<div class="bf-ncard-bars">';
  h+='<div class="bf-bar-row"><div class="bf-bar-meta"><span>RESERVE</span><span class="bf-bar-val">'+remainDisp+'</span></div><div class="bf-bar-track"><div class="bf-bar-fill '+ri.clr+'" style="width:'+reserveW+'%"></div></div></div>';
  h+='<div class="bf-bar-row"><div class="bf-bar-meta"><span>EXPIRY</span><span class="bf-bar-val">'+daysLabel+'</span></div><div class="bf-bar-track"><div class="bf-bar-fill '+ri.clr+'" style="width:'+expiryW+'%"></div></div></div>';
  h+='</div></div>';
  return h;
}

function rBillGroup(groupData){
  var contentEl=$('billContent');
  var dc=S._displayCurrency;var sym=S._currencySymbols[dc]||'$';
  var groupNames=Object.keys(groupData).sort(function(a,b){
    var at=0,bt=0;Object.values(groupData[a].totals).forEach(function(v){at+=v});Object.values(groupData[b].totals).forEach(function(v){bt+=v});return bt-at;
  });
  var h='';
  groupNames.forEach(function(gName){
    var gd=groupData[gName];
    var gCost=0;
    if(dc!=='original'&&S._rates){
      Object.entries(gd.totals).forEach(function(e){var cv=convertCurrency(e[1],e[0],dc);gCost+=cv?cv.amount:e[1]});
    }else{
      Object.values(gd.totals).forEach(function(v){gCost+=v});
    }
    var gCostStr=gCost>0?sym+gCost.toFixed(2)+'/mo':'--';
    h+='<div class="bf-group-hdr"><span class="bf-group-name">'+esc(gName)+'</span><span class="bf-group-line"></span><span class="bf-group-stat">'+gd.rows.length+' NODES</span><span class="bf-group-cost">'+gCostStr+'</span></div>';
    gd.rows.sort(function(a,b){return b.billing.monthly-a.billing.monthly});
    gd.rows.forEach(function(r){h+=nodeCardHtml(r)});
  });
  contentEl.innerHTML=h;
}

function rBillFlat(nodeRows){
  var contentEl=$('billContent');
  nodeRows.sort(function(a,b){return b.billing.monthly-a.billing.monthly});
  var h='';
  nodeRows.forEach(function(r){h+=nodeCardHtml(r)});
  contentEl.innerHTML=h;
}

function updateFleetCost(){
  var totals={};
  S.nodes.forEach(function(n){
    if(n.hidden)return;
    var b=fBilling(n);
    if(b.monthly>0&&b.currency){
      if(!totals[b.currency])totals[b.currency]=0;
      totals[b.currency]+=b.monthly;
    }
  });
  var el=$('fCost');if(!el)return;
  var entries=Object.entries(totals);
  if(entries.length===0){el.textContent='--';return}
  function fmtCost(v){if(v>=1e9)return(v/1e9).toFixed(1)+'B';if(v>=1e6)return(v/1e6).toFixed(1)+'M';if(v>=1e4)return(v/1e3).toFixed(1)+'K';return v.toFixed(0)}
  /* Convert all currencies to USD for unified display */
  if(entries.length===1){el.textContent=entries[0][0]+fmtCost(entries[0][1])+'/mo';return}
  if(S._rates){
    var usdTotal=0;
    entries.forEach(function(e){
      var c=convertCurrency(e[1],e[0],'USD');
      usdTotal+=c?c.amount:e[1];
    });
    el.textContent='$'+fmtCost(usdTotal)+'/mo';
  }else{
    fetchRates().then(function(){updateFleetCost()});
    el.textContent='...';
  }
}

/* ── Node Poster Export ── */
function exportNodePoster(uuid){
  var node=S.nodes.find(function(n){return n.uuid===uuid});if(!node)return;
  var b=fBilling(node);var on=S.onlineSet.has(uuid);var d=S.liveData[uuid]||{};
  var name=node.name||uuid,region=node.region||'',group=node.group||'';
  var os=d.os||node.os||'--',cpuModel=node.cpu_name||'--',cores=node.cpu_cores||'--';
  var ramTotal=fB(d.memory_total||node.mem_total||0),diskTotal=fB(d.disk_total||node.disk_total||0);
  var _pl=parseLabels(node);
  var trafficLimit=node.traffic_limit&&node.traffic_limit>0?fB(node.traffic_limit):(_pl.traffic||'不限');
  var netSpeed=node.network_speed&&node.network_speed>0?(node.network_speed>=1000?(node.network_speed/1000)+'Gbps':node.network_speed+'Mbps'):(_pl.bandwidth||'--');
  var priceStr=b.str||'--';
  var monthlyStr=b.monthly>0?b.currency+Math.round(b.monthly):'--';
  var cycleStr='--';
  if(node.billing_cycle){var cd=parseInt(node.billing_cycle);if(cd<=31)cycleStr='月付';else if(cd<=93)cycleStr='季付';else if(cd<=186)cycleStr='半年付';else if(cd<=366)cycleStr='年付';else cycleStr=Math.round(cd/365)+'年付';}
  var expDate=node.expired_at||'--';
  if(expDate!=='--'){try{var ed0=new Date(expDate);expDate=ed0.getFullYear()+'-'+String(ed0.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')+'-'+String(ed0.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')}catch(e){}}
  var remainStr='--',remainDays='';
  if(node.expired_at&&b.monthly>0){
    var ed=new Date(node.expired_at),nw=new Date();
    var rd=Math.max(0,Math.ceil((ed-nw)/(1000*60*60*24)));
    var cdd=parseInt(node.billing_cycle)||30;var rv=(rd/cdd)*node.price;
    remainStr=b.currency+Math.round(rv);remainDays=rd+'天';
  }
  var today=new Date();
  var dateStr=today.getFullYear()+'.'+String(today.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')+'.'+String(today.getDate()).padStart(2,'0');
  var siteName=S.sitename||'KOMARI';
  var charUrl='./char.png';
  if(S.themeSettings&&S.themeSettings.char_url)charUrl=S.themeSettings.char_url;

  var dotsH='';for(var i=0;i<45;i++){var sz=2+Math.random()*5;dotsH+='<div class="pp-dot" style="left:'+(25+Math.random()*75)+'%;top:'+Math.random()*100+'%;width:'+sz+'px;height:'+sz+'px;opacity:'+(0.08+Math.random()*0.42)+'"></div>'}

  var wrap=document.createElement('div');wrap.className='pw';
  wrap.innerHTML='<div class="pp">'+
    '<div class="pp-glow-r"></div><div class="pp-glow-top"></div>'+
    '<img class="pp-char" src="'+charUrl+'" crossorigin="anonymous" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">'+
    '<img class="pp-char-blur" src="'+charUrl+'" crossorigin="anonymous" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">'+
    '<div class="pp-frost"></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-scan"></div><div class="pp-dots">'+dotsH+'</div>'+
    '<div class="pp-frame"></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-cn tl"></div><div class="pp-cn tr"></div><div class="pp-cn bl"></div><div class="pp-cn br"></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-cdot" style="top:13px;left:13px"></div><div class="pp-cdot" style="top:13px;right:13px"></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-cdot" style="bottom:13px;left:13px"></div><div class="pp-cdot" style="bottom:13px;right:13px"></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-lt"></div><div class="pp-lb"></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-hud"><div class="pp-hud-t">[ NANO CORE ]</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-hud-r"><span class="pp-hd g"></span>SYNC CHANNEL LOCKED</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-hud-r"><span class="pp-hd g"></span>SIGNAL STABLE</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-hud-r"><span class="pp-hd b"></span>ENCRYPTION AES-256</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-hud-r"><span class="pp-hd b"></span>UPLINK ACTIVE</div></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-acc"><div class="pp-acc-l">IDENTITY VERIFIED</div><div class="pp-acc-l">BIOMETRIC MATCH 100%</div><div class="pp-acc-m">ACCESS GRANTED</div></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-orb"><div class="pp-or1"></div><div class="pp-or2"></div>'+
      '<div class="pp-od" style="top:6%;left:50%"></div><div class="pp-od" style="top:50%;right:0"></div>'+
      '<div class="pp-od" style="bottom:12%;left:18%"></div><div class="pp-od" style="top:28%;left:3%"></div></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-cross"><div class="pp-cross-d"></div></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-micro"><div class="pp-micro-l">NODE.UUID '+uuid.substring(0,8)+'</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-micro-l">TLS 1.3 · SECURE CHANNEL</div></div>'+
    '<div class="pp-ct">'+
      '<div class="pp-site"><svg width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#00d8ff" stroke-width="1.5"><path d="M12 2L2 7l10 5 10-5-10-5z"/><path d="M2 17l10 5 10-5"/><path d="M2 12l10 5 10-5"/></svg>'+esc(siteName)+'</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-title">'+esc(name)+'</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-sub">NANO CORE · SERVER PROFILE</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-chips">'+(region?'<span class="pp-chip">'+esc(region)+'</span>':'')+(group?'<span class="pp-chip">'+esc(group)+'</span>':'')+'<span class="pp-chip">'+esc(os.split(' ')[0]+' '+(os.split(' ')[1]||''))+'</span><span class="pp-st '+(on?'on':'off')+'">'+(on?'● ONLINE':'● OFFLINE')+'</span></div>'+
      '<div class="pp-specs">'+
        '<div class="pp-card"><div class="pp-ci">⚙</div><div><div class="pp-cl">CPU</div><div class="pp-cv">'+esc(cpuModel)+'</div></div></div>'+
        '<div class="pp-card"><div class="pp-ci">⬡</div><div><div class="pp-cl">CORES · RAM</div><div class="pp-cv">'+cores+'C · '+ramTotal+'</div></div></div>'+
        '<div class="pp-card"><div class="pp-ci">◈</div><div><div class="pp-cl">STORAGE</div><div class="pp-cv">'+diskTotal+' SSD</div></div></div>'+
        '<div class="pp-card"><div class="pp-ci">⇅</div><div><div class="pp-cl">TRAFFIC · BANDWIDTH</div><div class="pp-cv">'+trafficLimit+' · '+netSpeed+'</div></div></div>'+
      '</div>'+
      '<div class="pp-bot">'+
        '<div class="pp-box"><div class="pp-bl">MONTHLY COST</div><div class="pp-bv blue">'+esc(monthlyStr)+'<span class="pp-bu">/月</span></div><div class="pp-bs">'+esc(cycleStr)+' · '+esc(priceStr)+'</div></div>'+
        (remainStr!=='--'?'<div class="pp-box"><div class="pp-bl">REMAINING VALUE</div><div class="pp-bv green">'+esc(remainStr)+'</div><div class="pp-bs">到期 '+esc(expDate)+' · '+remainDays+'</div></div>':'')+
      '</div>'+
    '</div>'+
    '<div class="pp-ft"><span>NanoMuse · '+dateStr+'</span><span class="fr">SECURE · VERIFIED</span></div>'+
  '</div>';

  document.body.appendChild(wrap);
  var charImgEl=wrap.querySelector('.pp-char');
  function doCapture(){
    html2canvas(wrap.querySelector('.pp'),{scale:1,useCORS:true,allowTaint:true,backgroundColor:null,logging:false,width:1920,height:1080}).then(function(canvas){
      var link=document.createElement('a');
      link.download='NanoMuse-'+name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9\u4e00-\u9fff-]/g,'_')+'.png';
      link.href=canvas.toDataURL('image/png');link.click();
      document.body.removeChild(wrap);
    }).catch(function(err){console.error('Poster export failed:',err);document.body.removeChild(wrap)});
  }
  if(charImgEl&&charImgEl.naturalWidth===0){
    charImgEl.onload=function(){setTimeout(doCapture,150)};
    charImgEl.onerror=function(){setTimeout(doCapture,150)};
    setTimeout(doCapture,3000);
  }else{setTimeout(doCapture,200)}
}

/* ── Particles ── */
function initParticles(){
  const c=$('ptLayer');if(!c)return;
  for(let i=0;i<15;i++){
    const p=document.createElement('div');p.className='particle';
    const s=2+Math.random()*3;
    p.style.cssText=`left:${Math.random()*100}%;top:${Math.random()*100}%;width:${s}px;height:${s}px;animation-delay:${Math.random()*6}s;animation-duration:${4+Math.random()*4}s`;
    c.appendChild(p);
  }
}
/* ── Heartbeat ── */
function initHeartbeat(){
  if(S._hbInterval){clearInterval(S._hbInterval);S._hbInterval=null}
  const cv=$('hbCanvas');if(!cv)return;
  const ctx=cv.getContext('2d');
  const W=cv.width,H=cv.height;
  const pts=50;
  const txData=[],rxData=[];
  for(let i=0;i<pts;i++){txData.push(0);rxData.push(0)}

  function sample(){
    let txSum=0,rxSum=0,cnt=0;
    S.nodes.forEach(n=>{
      if(!S.onlineSet.has(n.uuid))return;
      const d=S.liveData[n.uuid];if(!d)return;
      txSum+=(d.network_tx||0);rxSum+=(d.network_rx||0);cnt++;
    });
    txData.push(txSum);if(txData.length>pts)txData.shift();
    rxData.push(rxSum);if(rxData.length>pts)rxData.shift();
  }

  function draw(){
    ctx.clearRect(0,0,W,H);
    const allVals=[...txData,...rxData];
    const maxV=Math.max(1,...allVals);
    const stepX=W/(pts-1);

    function drawLine(data,color,alpha,fillAlpha){
      ctx.beginPath();
      data.forEach((v,i)=>{
        const x=i*stepX;
        const y=H-8-(v/maxV)*(H-16);
        if(i===0)ctx.moveTo(x,y);
        else{
          const px=(i-1)*stepX,py=H-8-(data[i-1]/maxV)*(H-16);
          const cpx=(px+x)/2;
          ctx.bezierCurveTo(cpx,py,cpx,y,x,y);
        }
      });
      /* Fill under curve */
      ctx.strokeStyle=color;ctx.lineWidth=1.5*devicePixelRatio/2;ctx.globalAlpha=alpha;ctx.stroke();
      /* Gradient fill */
      const last=data.length-1;
      ctx.lineTo(last*stepX,H);ctx.lineTo(0,H);ctx.closePath();
      const grad=ctx.createLinearGradient(0,0,0,H);
      grad.addColorStop(0,color);grad.addColorStop(1,'rgba(0,0,0,0)');
      ctx.fillStyle=grad;ctx.globalAlpha=fillAlpha;ctx.fill();
      ctx.globalAlpha=1;
    }

    /* TX line (upload — green) */
    drawLine(txData,'rgba(34,197,94,0.8)',0.9,0.08);
    /* RX line (download — blue) */
    drawLine(rxData,'rgba(37,99,235,0.7)',0.7,0.06);

    /* Current value dot on TX */
    if(txData.length>1){
      const lastV=txData[txData.length-1];
      const lx=(txData.length-1)*stepX,ly=H-8-(lastV/maxV)*(H-16);
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(lx,ly,3,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.fillStyle='rgba(34,197,94,0.9)';ctx.fill();
      ctx.beginPath();ctx.arc(lx,ly,6,0,Math.PI*2);
      ctx.strokeStyle='rgba(34,197,94,0.3)';ctx.lineWidth=1;ctx.stroke();
    }
  }

  S._hbInterval=setInterval(()=>{sample();draw()},3000);
  sample();draw();
}


/* ── Copy node info to clipboard ── */
window.jumpNexus=function(){
  var uuid=S.detailUUID||'';
  window.location.href=uuid?'/nexus.html#'+uuid:'/nexus.html';
};
window.copyNodeInfo=function(){
  var uuid=S.detailUUID;if(!uuid)return;
  var n=S.detailNode||{};var d=S.liveData[uuid]||{};
  var on=S.onlineSet.has(uuid);
  var b=fBilling(n);
  var lines=[];
  lines.push('节点: '+(n.name||uuid));
  lines.push('状态: '+(on?'ONLINE':'OFFLINE'));
  if(n.region)lines.push('区域: '+n.region);
  if(n.group)lines.push('分组: '+n.group);
  if(d.os||n.os)lines.push('系统: '+(d.os||n.os));
  if(n.cpu_cores)lines.push('CPU: '+n.cpu_cores+' Cores');
  if(d.memory_total||n.mem_total)lines.push('内存: '+fB(d.memory_total||n.mem_total||0));
  if(d.disk_total||n.disk_total)lines.push('硬盘: '+fB(d.disk_total||n.disk_total||0));
  if(n.ipv4)lines.push('IPv4: '+n.ipv4);
  if(n.ipv6)lines.push('IPv6: '+n.ipv6);
  if(b.str)lines.push('费用: '+b.str);
  if(n.expired_at)lines.push('到期: '+n.expired_at.slice(0,10));
  if(n.traffic_limit&&n.traffic_limit>0)lines.push('流量: '+fB(n.traffic_limit));
  var text=lines.join('\n');
  navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(function(){
    var btn=document.querySelector('.det-copy-btn');
    if(btn){btn.textContent='COPIED ✓';btn.classList.add('copied');setTimeout(function(){btn.textContent='COPY INFO';btn.classList.remove('copied')},1500)}
  }).catch(function(){});
};

/* ── Expiry Calendar ── */
S._calMonth=new Date().getMonth();
S._calYear=new Date().getFullYear();

function renderCalendar(){
  var el=$('billCalendar');if(!el)return;
  var y=S._calYear,m=S._calMonth;
  var first=new Date(y,m,1);
  var last=new Date(y,m+1,0);
  var startDow=first.getDay();/* 0=Sun */
  var daysInMonth=last.getDate();
  var today=new Date();
  var isThisMonth=today.getFullYear()===y&&today.getMonth()===m;
  var todayDate=today.getDate();

  /* Build expiry map: day → [{name,days_left}] */
  var expMap={};
  S.nodes.forEach(function(n){
    if(!n.expired_at||n.hidden)return;
    var ed=new Date(n.expired_at);
    if(ed.getFullYear()===y&&ed.getMonth()===m){
      var day=ed.getDate();
      if(!expMap[day])expMap[day]=[];
      var dl=Math.max(0,Math.ceil((ed-today)/(86400000)));
      expMap[day].push({name:n.name||n.uuid,days:dl});
    }
  });

  var months=['1月','2月','3月','4月','5月','6月','7月','8月','9月','10月','11月','12月'];
  var h='<div class="bill-cal-hd"><span class="bill-cal-title">◇ '+y+'年'+months[m]+' · 到期日历</span>';
  h+='<div class="bill-cal-nav"><button onclick="calNav(-1)">◀</button><button onclick="calNav(0)">今</button><button onclick="calNav(1)">▶</button></div></div>';
  h+='<div class="bill-cal-grid">';
  ['日','一','二','三','四','五','六'].forEach(function(d){h+='<div class="bill-cal-dow">'+d+'</div>'});

  /* Empty cells before first day */
  for(var i=0;i<startDow;i++)h+='<div class="bill-cal-day empty"></div>';

  for(var d=1;d<=daysInMonth;d++){
    var cls='bill-cal-day';
    var exps=expMap[d];
    if(isThisMonth&&d===todayDate)cls+=' today';
    if(exps){
      var urgent=exps.some(function(e){return e.days<=7});
      cls+=urgent?' urgent':' has-exp';
    }
    h+='<div class="'+cls+'">'+d;
    if(exps){
      h+='<div class="bill-cal-dots">';
      exps.forEach(function(e){
        var c=e.days<=3?'#ef4444':e.days<=7?'#ea8420':e.days<=14?'#eab308':'#2563eb';
        h+='<div class="bill-cal-dot" style="background:'+c+'"></div>';
      });
      h+='</div>';
      h+='<div class="bill-cal-tip">'+exps.map(function(e){return e.name+(e.days<=0?' (已过期)':' · '+e.days+'天后')}).join('<br>')+'</div>';
    }
    h+='</div>';
  }
  h+='</div>';
  el.innerHTML=h;
}

window.calNav=function(dir){
  if(dir===0){S._calMonth=new Date().getMonth();S._calYear=new Date().getFullYear()}
  else{S._calMonth+=dir;if(S._calMonth>11){S._calMonth=0;S._calYear++}if(S._calMonth<0){S._calMonth=11;S._calYear--}}
  renderCalendar();
};
/* ── Init ── */
/* ── Character parallax: fade + drift on scroll ── */
function initCharParallax(){
  const char=document.querySelector('.anime-bg');
  const veil=document.querySelector('.char-veil');
  if(!char)return;
  if(char.dataset.videoHidden==='1')return;
  const hero=document.querySelector('.hero-top');
  if(!hero)return;
  let ticking=false;
  window.addEventListener('scroll',()=>{
    if(ticking)return;ticking=true;
    requestAnimationFrame(()=>{
      if(char.dataset.videoHidden==='1'){ticking=false;return}
      const sy=window.scrollY;
      const hH=hero.offsetHeight||600;
      const t40=hH*0.35, t80=hH*0.75;
      /* Parallax drift: very subtle */
      const drift=sy*0.06;
      /* Opacity: 1 → 0.12 between 35%-75% of hero, then → 0.03 */
      let op=1;
      if(sy>t40){
        const prog=Math.min(1,(sy-t40)/(t80-t40));
        op=1-prog*0.88; /* 1 → 0.12 */
      }
      if(sy>t80){
        const prog2=Math.min(1,(sy-t80)/(hH*0.3));
        op=0.12-prog2*0.09; /* 0.12 → 0.03 */
      }
      op=Math.max(0.03,op);
      /* Blur: 0 → 2px as she fades */
      const blur=Math.min(2,(1-op)*2.5);
      char.style.transform=`translateX(-50%) translateY(${drift.toFixed(1)}px)`;
      char.style.opacity=op.toFixed(3);
      char.style.filter=`brightness(1.02) blur(${blur.toFixed(1)}px)`;
      if(veil)veil.style.opacity=op.toFixed(3);
      ticking=false;
    });
  },{passive:true});
}

/* ── Terminal Link: visitor IP geolocation ── */
S.termData=null;
async function fetchTermLink(){
  try{
    let d=null;
    try{
      const r=await fetch('https://ipapi.co/json/');const raw=await r.json();
      if(raw&&raw.ip){d={ip:raw.ip,country:raw.country_name,cc:raw.country_code,city:raw.city,region:raw.region_code||raw.region,regionFull:raw.region,isp:raw.org||'--',asn:raw.asn||'--',lat:raw.latitude,lon:raw.longitude,tz:raw.timezone||'--',currency:raw.currency||'--',languages:raw.languages||'--',utc:raw.utc_offset||'--',postal:raw.postal||'--'}}
    }catch(e){
      try{const r2=await fetch('https://ipwho.is/');const raw2=await r2.json();
        if(raw2&&raw2.ip){d={ip:raw2.ip,country:raw2.country,cc:raw2.country_code,city:raw2.city,region:raw2.region,regionFull:raw2.region,isp:raw2.connection?.org||'--',asn:raw2.connection?.asn||'--',tz:raw2.timezone?.id||'--',lat:raw2.latitude,lon:raw2.longitude}}
      }catch(e2){}
    }
    if(!d||!d.ip)return;
    const ua=navigator.userAgent||'';
    const brw=parseUA(ua);
    d.browser=brw.browser;d.os=brw.os;d.ua=ua;
    d.screen=screen.width+'×'+screen.height;
    d.lang=navigator.language||'--';
    d.cores=navigator.hardwareConcurrency||'--';
    d.conn=(navigator.connection?.effectiveType||'--').toUpperCase();
    d.flag=countryFlag(d.cc);
    S.termData=d;
    const fl=$('tlFlag');if(fl)fl.textContent=d.flag;
    const loc=$('tlLoc');if(loc)loc.textContent='Welcome, '+(d.city||d.region||'--');
    const locF=$('tlLocFull');if(locF)locF.textContent=(d.country||'--')+', '+(d.regionFull||d.region||'--')+', '+(d.city||'--');
    const ipE=$('tlIP');if(ipE)ipE.textContent=d.ip;
    const asnE=$('tlASN');if(asnE)asnE.textContent=d.asn+', '+d.isp;
    const brE=$('tlBrowser');if(brE)brE.textContent=d.browser;
    const osE=$('tlOS');if(osE)osE.textContent=d.os;
    /* proxycheck.io risk detection — requires key from theme_settings */
    var pcKey=(S.themeSettings&&S.themeSettings.proxycheck_key)?S.themeSettings.proxycheck_key.trim():'';
    if(pcKey){
      try{
        const qr=await fetch('https://proxycheck.io/v2/?key='+encodeURIComponent(pcKey)+'&vpn=1&asn=1&risk=1');
        const q=await qr.json();
        var rip=q.ip||d.ip;
        if(q&&(q.status==='ok'||q.status==='warning')&&q[rip]){
          var r=q[rip];
          const typeEl=$('tlType');
          if(typeEl){
            var tags=[];
            var ct=r.type||'';
            if(ct)tags.push('<span class="tl-tag tl-tag-info">'+ct+'</span>');
            if(r.proxy==='yes')tags.push('<span class="tl-tag tl-tag-warn">Proxy</span>');
            if(r.vpn==='yes')tags.push('<span class="tl-tag tl-tag-warn">VPN</span>');
            if(r.proxy!=='yes'&&r.vpn!=='yes')tags.push('<span class="tl-tag tl-tag-safe">Clean</span>');
            typeEl.innerHTML=tags.join(' ');
          }
          const riskEl=$('tlRisk');
          if(riskEl){
            var score=parseInt(r.risk)||0;
            var cls=score<=33?'tl-tag-safe':score<=66?'tl-tag-warn':'tl-tag-danger';
            var label=score<=33?'Low':score<=66?'Medium':'High';
            riskEl.innerHTML='<span class="tl-tag '+cls+'">'+score+'/100 '+label+'</span>';
          }
        }
      }catch(eq){console.log('[NM] proxycheck failed',eq)}
    }else{
      /* No key — hide TYPE and RISK rows */
      var typeEl=$('tlType');if(typeEl)typeEl.closest('.tl-row').style.display='none';
      var riskEl=$('tlRisk');if(riskEl)riskEl.closest('.tl-row').style.display='none';
    }
  }catch(e){console.log('[NM] Terminal link failed',e)}
}
function parseUA(ua){
  let browser='Unknown',os='Unknown';
  if(/Edg\/([\d.]+)/.test(ua))browser='Edge '+RegExp.$1;
  else if(/OPR\/([\d.]+)/.test(ua))browser='Opera '+RegExp.$1;
  else if(/Chrome\/([\d.]+)/.test(ua))browser='Chrome '+RegExp.$1;
  else if(/Firefox\/([\d.]+)/.test(ua))browser='Firefox '+RegExp.$1;
  else if(/Safari\/([\d.]+)/.test(ua)&&/Version\/([\d.]+)/.test(ua))browser='Safari '+RegExp.$1;
  if(/Windows NT ([\d.]+)/.test(ua)){var v=RegExp.$1;os='Windows'+(v==='10.0'?' 10/11':v==='6.3'?' 8.1':v==='6.1'?' 7':' '+v)}
  else if(/Mac OS X ([\d_]+)/.test(ua))os='macOS '+RegExp.$1.replace(/_/g,'.');
  else if(/Android ([\d.]+)/.test(ua))os='Android '+RegExp.$1;
  else if(/iPhone OS ([\d_]+)/.test(ua))os='iOS '+RegExp.$1.replace(/_/g,'.');
  else if(/Linux/.test(ua))os='Linux';
  return{browser:browser,os:os};
}
function countryFlag(cc){
  if(!cc||cc.length!==2)return'🌐';
  const f=String.fromCodePoint(...[...cc.toUpperCase()].map(c=>0x1F1E6+c.charCodeAt(0)-65));
  return f;
}
function renderTLModal(){
  const d=S.termData;if(!d)return;
  const g=$('tlGreeting');
  if(g)g.textContent='Welcome, '+(d.city||d.regionFull||'--');
  const body=$('tlModalBody');if(!body)return;
  function mrow(icon,label,val){return '<div class="tl-modal-row"><span class="tl-modal-icon">'+icon+'</span><span class="tl-modal-label">'+label+'</span><span class="tl-modal-val">'+val+'</span></div>'}
  function mtag(text,cls){return '<span class="tl-modal-tag '+cls+'">'+text+'</span>'}
  var h='';
  h+=mrow('📍','Location:',esc((d.country||'--')+', '+(d.regionFull||d.region||'--')+', '+(d.city||'--')));
  h+=mrow('🖥','IP:',esc(d.ip));
  h+=mrow('✦','ASN:',esc(d.asn+', '+d.isp));
  h+=mrow('🌐','Browser:',esc(d.browser)+' ('+esc(d.os)+')');
  h+=mrow('📱','Display:',d.screen+' · '+d.cores+' Cores');
  h+=mrow('🌍','Timezone:',esc(d.tz||'--')+(d.utc?' (UTC'+d.utc+')':''));
  h+=mrow('🗣','Lang:',esc(d.lang));
  if(d.conn&&d.conn!=='--')h+=mrow('📶','Network:',d.conn);
  if(d.currency&&d.currency!=='--')h+=mrow('💰','Currency:',d.currency);
  var ispLow=(d.isp||'').toLowerCase();
  var ipType='Residential',typeClass='green';
  if(/cloud|hosting|server|data.?cent|hetzner|ovh|vultr|digital.?ocean|amazon|google|azure|linode|choopa/i.test(ispLow)){ipType='Datacenter';typeClass='amber'}
  else if(/mobile|cellular|wireless/i.test(ispLow)){ipType='Mobile';typeClass='blue'}
  h+=mrow('🏷','IP Type:',mtag(ipType,typeClass));
  h+=mrow('✅','Status:',mtag('Clean','green'));
  body.innerHTML=h;
}
(function(){
  var wrap=$('termLinkWrap'),modal=$('tlModal'),close=$('tlModalClose');
  if(wrap)wrap.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();if(S.termData)renderTLModal();if(modal)modal.classList.add('show')});
  if(close)close.addEventListener('click',function(e){e.stopPropagation();if(modal)modal.classList.remove('show')});
  if(modal)modal.addEventListener('click',function(e){if(e.target===modal)modal.classList.remove('show')});
})();

async function init(){
  try{
    const booted=sessionStorage.getItem('nm-booted');
    if(booted){
      const ov=$('bootOverlay');if(ov)ov.style.display='none';
      document.body.classList.remove('booting');
      document.body.classList.add('boot-skip');
    }
    /* Start boot animation IMMEDIATELY */
    const bootPromise=booted?Promise.resolve():bootSequence();
    /* Fetch data in parallel */
    await Promise.all([fetchP(),fetchN(),fetchMe()]);
    rGF();render();conWS();hRoute();
    initParticles();initHeartbeat();fetchTermLink();
    /* Character parallax fade on scroll */
    initCharParallax();
    /* Wait for boot to finish */
    await bootPromise;
    if(!booted){
      document.body.classList.remove('booting');
      document.body.classList.add('boot-done');
      const overlay=$('bootOverlay');
      if(overlay)overlay.classList.add('done');
      sessionStorage.setItem('nm-booted','1');
    }
    rSum();
  }catch(e){
    console.error('Init failed:',e);
    document.body.classList.remove('booting');
    document.body.classList.add('boot-skip');
    const overlay=$('bootOverlay');
    if(overlay){overlay.classList.add('done')}
  }
}
function bootSequence(){
  return new Promise(resolve=>{
    const bootRing=$('bootRing');const bootPct=$('bootPct');
    const statusEl=$('bootStatus');
    const overlay=$('bootOverlay');
    const twText=$('bootTwText');
    const twWrap=$('bootTypewriter');
    const ringWrap=$('bootRingWrap');
    const scanline=$('bootScanline');
    const completeEl=$('bootComplete');
    const bootCirc=2*Math.PI*120;

    /* ── Phase A (0–0.8s): Typewriter on deep cold blue-gray ── */
    const twString='INITIALIZING NANO CORE';
    const charDelay=36; /* faster: ~0.8s total for 22 chars */
    let charIdx=0;

    /* Scan line sweeps during typewriter */
    if(scanline){
      scanline.style.opacity='1';
      scanline.style.transition='top 1.2s ease-in-out';
      scanline.style.top='100%';
    }

    function typeNext(){
      if(charIdx<twString.length){
        twText.textContent+=twString[charIdx];
        charIdx++;
        setTimeout(typeNext,charDelay);
      }else{
        /* Phase B (0.8–1.0s): seamless crossfade to ring — NO pause */
        startProgress();
      }
    }

    /* ── Phase B→C: Ring progress (~2s) + overlay fade ── */
    function startProgress(){
      /* Crossfade: typewriter out, ring in */
      twWrap.style.transition='opacity 0.3s ease';
      twWrap.style.opacity='0';
      ringWrap.style.transition='opacity 0.5s ease, transform 0.5s ease';
      ringWrap.style.opacity='1';
      ringWrap.style.transform='scale(1)';
      statusEl.style.transition='opacity 0.3s ease';
      statusEl.style.opacity='1';

      const duration=2000; /* tighter: 2s instead of 3s */
      const start=performance.now();
      const phases=[
        {at:0,text:'SYNCHRONIZING ...'},
        {at:0.35,text:'LINKING NODE ARRAY ...'},
        {at:0.65,text:'CALIBRATING ...'},
        {at:0.88,text:'CORE ONLINE'}
      ];
      let phaseIdx=0;

      function tick(now){
        const elapsed=now-start;const progress=Math.min(elapsed/duration,1);
        const eased=progress<0.5?2*progress*progress:1-Math.pow(-2*progress+2,2)/2;
        const target=88;
        const current=target*eased;

        if(bootRing)bootRing.style.strokeDashoffset=(bootCirc-(bootCirc*current/100)).toFixed(1);
        if(bootPct)bootPct.textContent=Math.round(current)+'%';

        while(phaseIdx<phases.length&&progress>=phases[phaseIdx].at){
          if(statusEl)statusEl.textContent=phases[phaseIdx].text;
          phaseIdx++;
        }

        /* Overlay: girl stays in "cold fog" during boot — NOT fully revealed
           Boot is "preheating", not the climax. Girl should be a silhouette/muted.
           0% → 0.97 (deep fog)
           50% → 0.60 (silhouette emerging)
           100% → 0.30 (visible but veiled — restrained, energy stays low)
           Real reveal happens when overlay removes entirely at boot-done */
        if(overlay){
          const overlayOpacity=Math.max(0.30, 0.97 - progress * 0.72);
          overlay.style.background=`rgba(14,26,34,${overlayOpacity.toFixed(3)})`;
          if(progress>0.7){
            const ringFade=1-((progress-0.7)/0.3);
            const statusTxt=overlay.querySelector('.boot-status');
            if(ringWrap)ringWrap.style.opacity=ringFade.toFixed(2);
            if(statusTxt)statusTxt.style.opacity=ringFade.toFixed(2);
          }
        }

        if(progress<1){requestAnimationFrame(tick)}
        else{
          /* ── Phase D: Completion ceremony ── */
          completeBoot();
        }
      }
      requestAnimationFrame(tick);
    }

    /* ── Phase D: 88% completion — brief energy burst then system online ── */
    function completeBoot(){
      /* Pulse the ring with glow burst */
      if(ringWrap){
        ringWrap.style.transition='none';
        ringWrap.style.opacity='1';
        ringWrap.style.animation='boot-pulse 0.3s ease';
        ringWrap.style.filter='drop-shadow(0 0 30px rgba(0,216,255,0.6))';
      }
      /* Flash SYNC COMPLETE */
      if(completeEl){
        completeEl.style.animation='complete-flash 0.6s ease forwards';
      }
      /* Brief glow on overlay then clear — the "fog lifts" moment */
      if(overlay){
        overlay.style.transition='background 0.4s ease';
        overlay.style.background='rgba(14,26,34,0.10)';
        setTimeout(()=>{
          overlay.style.background='rgba(14,26,34,0)';
        },200);
      }
      if(statusEl)statusEl.style.opacity='0';
      /* Resolve after ceremony */
      setTimeout(resolve,500);
    }

    typeNext();
  });
}
function render(){rSum();rCards()}

var WMAP_COORDS_CACHE={};
var WMAP_SPREAD_COUNT={};
function wmapSpread(lat,lng,idx,radius){
if(idx===0)return{lat:lat,lng:lng};
var angle=(idx-1)*2.399;var ring=Math.ceil(idx/6);var r=radius*ring*0.6;
return{lat:lat+Math.sin(angle)*r,lng:lng+Math.cos(angle)*r};
}

function wmapProject(lat,lng,w,h){
var LAT_MIN=-60,LAT_MAX=83;lat=Math.max(LAT_MIN,Math.min(LAT_MAX,lat));
var x=((lng+180)/360)*960;var latRad=lat*Math.PI/180;
var m=Math.log(Math.tan(Math.PI/4+latRad/2));
var mMax=Math.log(Math.tan(Math.PI/4+(LAT_MAX*Math.PI/180)/2));
var mMin=Math.log(Math.tan(Math.PI/4+(LAT_MIN*Math.PI/180)/2));
var y=480*(mMax-m)/(mMax-mMin);
x=x*(w/960);y=y*(h/480);x=Math.max(5,Math.min(w-5,x));y=Math.max(5,Math.min(h-5,y));return{x:x,y:y};
}

/* Lightweight worldmap node status update — no DOM rebuild */
function wmapUpdateNodes(){
  var dots=document.querySelectorAll('.wmap-dot');
  dots.forEach(function(dot){
    var uuid=dot.getAttribute('data-uuid');
    if(!uuid)return;
    var on=S.onlineSet.has(uuid);
    dot.setAttribute('class','wmap-dot'+(on?' on':' off'));
  });
  /* Update node list online badges */
  var items=document.querySelectorAll('.wmap-node-item');
  items.forEach(function(item){
    var uuid=item.getAttribute('data-uuid');
    if(!uuid)return;
    var on=S.onlineSet.has(uuid);
    var badge=item.querySelector('.wmap-node-status');
    if(badge){badge.setAttribute('class','wmap-node-status'+(on?' on':' off'));badge.textContent=on?'ONLINE':'OFFLINE'}
  });
}
;WMAP_SPREAD_COUNT={};
var wrap=document.getElementById('wmap-svg-wrap');if(!wrap)return;
var W=960,H=480;
var svg='<svg viewBox="0 0 '+W+' '+H+'" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="background:transparent">';

for(var gi=1;gi<8;gi++){var gy=gi*(H/8);svg+='<line class="wmap-grid-line" x1="0" y1="'+gy+'" x2="'+W+'" y2="'+gy+'"/>';}
for(var gj=1;gj<16;gj++){var gx=gj*(W/16);svg+='<line class="wmap-grid-line" x1="'+gx+'" y1="0" x2="'+gx+'" y2="'+H+'"/>';}

svg+='<path class="wmap-land" d="'+WMAP_LAND+'"/>';
var mapNodes=[];

var mc=m.on?'rgba(0,216,255,0.9)':'rgba(255,77,79,0.7)';var po=m.on?'.12':'.04';

if(m.on)svg+='<circle cx="0" cy="0" r="2" fill="rgba(255,255,255,.4)"/>';

var _wmZ={scale:1,tx:0,ty:0,dragging:false,sx:0,sy:0,stx:0,sty:0};
var _wmG=document.getElementById('wmap-transform');
function _wmApply(){if(!_wmG)return;_wmG.setAttribute('transform','translate('+_wmZ.tx+','+_wmZ.ty+') scale('+_wmZ.scale+')');var inv=1/_wmZ.scale;_wmG.querySelectorAll('.wmap-node-group').forEach(function(g){var orig=g.getAttribute('data-pos');if(orig){var pp=orig.split(',');g.setAttribute('transform','translate('+pp[0]+','+pp[1]+') scale('+inv+')')}})}
function _wmZoomFn(delta,cx,cy){var os=_wmZ.scale;_wmZ.scale=Math.max(.5,Math.min(8,_wmZ.scale*(1+delta)));var ns=_wmZ.scale;if(cx!==undefined){_wmZ.tx=cx-(cx-_wmZ.tx)*ns/os;_wmZ.ty=cy-(cy-_wmZ.ty)*ns/os}_wmApply()}
wrap.addEventListener('wheel',function(e){e.preventDefault();var rect=wrap.querySelector('svg').getBoundingClientRect();var mx=(e.clientX-rect.left)/rect.width*W;var my=(e.clientY-rect.top)/rect.height*H;_wmZoomFn(e.deltaY>0?-0.12:0.12,mx,my)},{passive:false});
wrap.addEventListener('mousedown',function(e){if(e.button!==0)return;_wmZ.dragging=true;_wmZ.sx=e.clientX;_wmZ.sy=e.clientY;_wmZ.stx=_wmZ.tx;_wmZ.sty=_wmZ.ty;wrap.classList.add('dragging');e.preventDefault()});
document.addEventListener('mousemove',function(e){if(!_wmZ.dragging)return;var svgRect=wrap.querySelector('svg');if(!svgRect)return;var r=svgRect.getBoundingClientRect();_wmZ.tx=_wmZ.stx+(e.clientX-_wmZ.sx)*(W/r.width);_wmZ.ty=_wmZ.sty+(e.clientY-_wmZ.sy)*(W/r.width);_wmApply()});
document.addEventListener('mouseup',function(){if(_wmZ.dragging){_wmZ.dragging=false;wrap.classList.remove('dragging')}});
var _wmTouch={lastDist:0};
wrap.addEventListener('touchstart',function(e){if(e.touches.length===1){_wmZ.dragging=true;_wmZ.sx=e.touches[0].clientX;_wmZ.sy=e.touches[0].clientY;_wmZ.stx=_wmZ.tx;_wmZ.sty=_wmZ.ty}else if(e.touches.length===2){_wmTouch.lastDist=Math.hypot(e.touches[1].clientX-e.touches[0].clientX,e.touches[1].clientY-e.touches[0].clientY)}},{passive:true});
wrap.addEventListener('touchmove',function(e){if(e.touches.length===1&&_wmZ.dragging){var r=wrap.querySelector('svg').getBoundingClientRect();_wmZ.tx=_wmZ.stx+(e.touches[0].clientX-_wmZ.sx)*(W/r.width);_wmZ.ty=_wmZ.sty+(e.touches[0].clientY-_wmZ.sy)*(W/r.width);_wmApply()}else if(e.touches.length===2){var d=Math.hypot(e.touches[1].clientX-e.touches[0].clientX,e.touches[1].clientY-e.touches[0].clientY);if(_wmTouch.lastDist>0)_wmZoomFn((d-_wmTouch.lastDist)*0.005,W/2,H/2);_wmTouch.lastDist=d}e.preventDefault()},{passive:false});
wrap.addEventListener('touchend',function(){_wmZ.dragging=false;_wmTouch.lastDist=0},{passive:true});
var zi=document.getElementById('wmap-zoom-in');if(zi)zi.addEventListener('click',function(){_wmZoomFn(0.3,W/2,H/2)});
var zo=document.getElementById('wmap-zoom-out');if(zo)zo.addEventListener('click',function(){_wmZoomFn(-0.25,W/2,H/2)});
var zr=document.getElementById('wmap-zoom-reset');if(zr)zr.addEventListener('click',function(){_wmZ.scale=1;_wmZ.tx=0;_wmZ.ty=0;_wmApply()});
S._wmZoom=_wmZ;
if(S._wmZoomPrev){_wmZ.scale=S._wmZoomPrev.scale;_wmZ.tx=S._wmZoomPrev.tx;_wmZ.ty=S._wmZoomPrev.ty;_wmApply()}
/* Tooltips */
var tip=document.getElementById('wmap-tip');var container=document.getElementById('wmap-container');
wrap.querySelectorAll('.wmap-node-group').forEach(function(g){
g.addEventListener('mouseenter',function(e){var uuid=this.getAttribute('data-uuid');var n=S.nodes.find(function(nd){return nd.uuid===uuid});if(!n)return;var on=S.onlineSet.has(uuid);var l=S.liveData[uuid];var cpuStr='',memStr='';if(on&&l){cpuStr='CPU: '+(l.cpu||0).toFixed(1)+'%';memStr=' MEM: '+(l.ram||0).toFixed(1)+'%'}tip.innerHTML='<div class="wmap-tip-name">'+(n.region||'')+' '+esc(n.name)+'</div><div class="wmap-tip-status '+(on?'online':'offline')+'">◆ '+(on?'ONLINE':'OFFLINE')+'</div>'+(on?'<div class="wmap-tip-stats">'+cpuStr+memStr+'</div>':'');var rect=container.getBoundingClientRect();var gRect=this.getBoundingClientRect();tip.style.left=(gRect.left+gRect.width/2-rect.left)+'px';tip.style.top=(gRect.top-rect.top)+'px';tip.classList.add('show')});

/* Overview stats */
var ovEl=document.getElementById('wmap-overview');
if(ovEl){var total=S.nodes.filter(function(n){return!n.hidden}).length;var onCount=0;S.nodes.forEach(function(n){if(!n.hidden&&S.onlineSet.has(n.uuid))onCount++});var mapped=mapNodes.length;var groups={};mapNodes.forEach(function(m){var g=m.node.group||'Other';if(!groups[g])groups[g]=0;groups[g]++});var regionCount=Object.keys(groups).length;ovEl.innerHTML='<div class="fleet-cell"><div class="fleet-val" style="color:var(--cyan)">'+mapped+'<span style="font-size:11px;opacity:.5"> / '+total+'</span></div><div class="fleet-lbl">MAPPED NODES</div></div><div class="fleet-cell"><div class="fleet-val" style="color:var(--g)">'+onCount+'</div><div class="fleet-lbl">ONLINE</div></div><div class="fleet-cell"><div class="fleet-val" style="color:var(--r)">'+(total-onCount)+'</div><div class="fleet-lbl">OFFLINE</div></div><div class="fleet-cell"><div class="fleet-val" style="color:var(--am)">'+regionCount+'</div><div class="fleet-lbl">REGIONS</div></div>'}
